--- DATABASE: /var/www/xrlab/ka/data/ka_auth.db ---
Tables:
articles            question_claims     research_questions  submission_batches
audit_log           refresh_tokens      reset_tokens        users             

Full schema:
CREATE TABLE users (
        user_id     TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        email       TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        first_name  TEXT NOT NULL,
        last_name   TEXT NOT NULL,
        role        TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'student',
        password_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
        status      TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
        track       TEXT,
        question_id TEXT,
        institution TEXT DEFAULT 'UC San Diego',
        department  TEXT,
        created_at  TEXT NOT NULL,
        approved_at TEXT,
        last_login  TEXT
    );
CREATE TABLE reset_tokens (
        token       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        user_id     TEXT NOT NULL,
        expires_at  TEXT NOT NULL,
        used        INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
    );
CREATE TABLE refresh_tokens (
        token       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        user_id     TEXT NOT NULL,
        expires_at  TEXT NOT NULL,
        revoked     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
    );
CREATE TABLE research_questions (
        question_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        label       TEXT NOT NULL,
        domain      TEXT NOT NULL,
        text        TEXT NOT NULL,
        atlas_topic TEXT,
        notes       TEXT
    );
CREATE TABLE articles (
        article_id          TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        submission_id       TEXT NOT NULL,
        submitter_id        TEXT,
        submitter_type      TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'anonymous',
        track               TEXT,
        input_mode          TEXT NOT NULL,

        doi                 TEXT,
        title               TEXT,
        authors             TEXT,
        year                INTEGER,
        journal             TEXT,
        abstract            TEXT,
        citation_raw        TEXT,

        pdf_filename        TEXT,
        pdf_hash_sha256     TEXT,
        pdf_size_bytes      INTEGER,
        quarantine_path     TEXT,
        promoted_path       TEXT,

        article_type        TEXT,          -- experimental | review | theory | mechanism | meta_analysis | other | unknown
        a0_task             TEXT,          -- task1 (experimental-only) | task2 (any-type) | NULL (non-A0)
        article_type_valid  INTEGER DEFAULT 0,  -- 1 if type confirmed appropriate for the task

        status              TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'received',
        duplicate_of        TEXT,
        validation_notes    TEXT,
        relevance_score     REAL,
        review_notes        TEXT,

        assigned_question_id TEXT,
        topic_tags          TEXT,

        source_surface      TEXT DEFAULT 'ka_contribute',
        course_context      TEXT,
        submitter_notes     TEXT,

        created_at          TEXT NOT NULL,
        validated_at        TEXT,
        staged_at           TEXT,
        reviewed_at         TEXT,
        promoted_at         TEXT,
        rejected_at         TEXT,

        metadata_confidence TEXT DEFAULT 'low'
    );
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_status ON articles(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_submitter ON articles(submitter_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_doi ON articles(doi);
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_hash ON articles(pdf_hash_sha256);
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_submission ON articles(submission_id);
CREATE TABLE submission_batches (
        submission_id   TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        submitter_id    TEXT,
        submitter_type  TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'anonymous',
        input_mode      TEXT NOT NULL,
        item_count      INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
        source_surface  TEXT,
        created_at      TEXT NOT NULL,
        completed_at    TEXT
    );
CREATE TABLE audit_log (
        log_id      INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        article_id  TEXT NOT NULL,
        action      TEXT NOT NULL,
        old_status  TEXT,
        new_status  TEXT,
        actor_id    TEXT,
        actor_type  TEXT DEFAULT 'system',
        details     TEXT,
        created_at  TEXT NOT NULL
    );
CREATE TABLE sqlite_sequence(name,seq);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_article ON audit_log(article_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_action ON audit_log(action);
CREATE TABLE question_claims (
        claim_id        INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        question_id     TEXT NOT NULL,          -- FK → research_questions.question_id
        user_id         TEXT NOT NULL,           -- FK → users.user_id
        round           INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,  -- round 1, 2, 3, ...
        claimed_at      TEXT NOT NULL,
        released_at     TEXT,                    -- NULL if still held
        task1_count     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,  -- experimental articles submitted for this claim
        task2_count     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,  -- any-type articles submitted for this claim
        UNIQUE(question_id, round)               -- one claim per question per round
    );
CREATE INDEX idx_claims_user ON question_claims(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_claims_question ON question_claims(question_id, round);

--- DATABASE: /var/www/xrlab/ka/data/ka_auth.db ---
Tables:
articles            question_claims     research_questions  submission_batches

Full schema:
CREATE TABLE users (
        user_id     TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        email       TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        first_name  TEXT NOT NULL,
        last_name   TEXT NOT NULL,
        role        TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'student',
        password_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
        status      TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
        track       TEXT,
        question_id TEXT,
        institution TEXT DEFAULT 'UC San Diego',
        department  TEXT,
        created_at  TEXT NOT NULL,
        approved_at TEXT,
        last_login  TEXT
    );
CREATE TABLE reset_tokens (
        token       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        user_id     TEXT NOT NULL,
        expires_at  TEXT NOT NULL,
        used        INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
    );
CREATE TABLE refresh_tokens (
        token       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        user_id     TEXT NOT NULL,
        expires_at  TEXT NOT NULL,
        revoked     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
    );
CREATE TABLE research_questions (
        question_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        label       TEXT NOT NULL,
        domain      TEXT NOT NULL,
        text        TEXT NOT NULL,
        atlas_topic TEXT,
        notes       TEXT
    );
CREATE TABLE articles (
        article_id          TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        submission_id       TEXT NOT NULL,
        submitter_id        TEXT,
        submitter_type      TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'anonymous',
        track               TEXT,
        input_mode          TEXT NOT NULL,

        doi                 TEXT,
        title               TEXT,
        authors             TEXT,
        year                INTEGER,
        journal             TEXT,
        abstract            TEXT,
        citation_raw        TEXT,

        pdf_filename        TEXT,
        pdf_hash_sha256     TEXT,
        pdf_size_bytes      INTEGER,
        quarantine_path     TEXT,
        promoted_path       TEXT,

        article_type        TEXT,          -- experimental | review | theory | mechanism | meta_analysis | other | unknown
        a0_task             TEXT,          -- task1 (experimental-only) | task2 (any-type) | NULL (non-A0)
        article_type_valid  INTEGER DEFAULT 0,  -- 1 if type confirmed appropriate for the task

        status              TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'received',
        duplicate_of        TEXT,
        validation_notes    TEXT,
        relevance_score     REAL,
        review_notes        TEXT,

        assigned_question_id TEXT,
        topic_tags          TEXT,

        source_surface      TEXT DEFAULT 'ka_contribute',
        course_context      TEXT,
        submitter_notes     TEXT,

        created_at          TEXT NOT NULL,
        validated_at        TEXT,
        staged_at           TEXT,
        reviewed_at         TEXT,
        promoted_at         TEXT,
        rejected_at         TEXT,

        metadata_confidence TEXT DEFAULT 'low'
    );
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_status ON articles(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_submitter ON articles(submitter_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_doi ON articles(doi);
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_hash ON articles(pdf_hash_sha256);
CREATE INDEX idx_articles_submission ON articles(submission_id);
CREATE TABLE submission_batches (
        submission_id   TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        submitter_id    TEXT,
        submitter_type  TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'anonymous',
        input_mode      TEXT NOT NULL,
        item_count      INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
        source_surface  TEXT,
        created_at      TEXT NOT NULL,
        completed_at    TEXT
    );
CREATE TABLE audit_log (
        log_id      INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        article_id  TEXT NOT NULL,
        action      TEXT NOT NULL,
        old_status  TEXT,
        new_status  TEXT,
        actor_id    TEXT,
        actor_type  TEXT DEFAULT 'system',
        details     TEXT,
        created_at  TEXT NOT NULL
    );
CREATE TABLE sqlite_sequence(name,seq);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_article ON audit_log(article_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_action ON audit_log(action);
CREATE TABLE question_claims (
        claim_id        INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        question_id     TEXT NOT NULL,          -- FK → research_questions.question_id
        user_id         TEXT NOT NULL,           -- FK → users.user_id
        round           INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,  -- round 1, 2, 3, ...
        claimed_at      TEXT NOT NULL,
        released_at     TEXT,                    -- NULL if still held
        task1_count     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,  -- experimental articles submitted for this claim
        task2_count     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,  -- any-type articles submitted for this claim
        UNIQUE(question_id, round)               -- one claim per question per round
    );
CREATE INDEX idx_claims_user ON question_claims(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_claims_question ON question_claims(question_id, round);

            track_choice1 TEXT,
            track_choice2 TEXT,
            status TEXT,
            approved_track TEXT,
            rejection_reason TEXT,
            timestamp TEXT,
            approved_at TEXT,
            rejected_at TEXT
        );
CREATE TABLE intake_submissions (
            submission_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            user_id TEXT,
            identity_type TEXT,
            track TEXT,
            status TEXT,
            kind TEXT,
            title TEXT,
            citation TEXT,
            authors TEXT,
            abstract TEXT,
            created_at TEXT
        );
CREATE TABLE track_targets (
            track_label TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            target INTEGER NOT NULL
        );

<!-- ── Hero ── -->
<header class="hero">
  <p class="hero-eyebrow">COGS 160 · Spring 2026</p>
  <h1>Choose Your Track</h1>
  <p class="hero-sub">Four tracks, four capability gaps, one shared system. Each track produces real components that integrate into Knowledge Atlas. Browse the details below, then sign up.</p>
</header>

<div class="page-wrap">

  <!-- ── How Tracks Work ── -->
  <div class="section">
    <h2>How Tracks Work</h2>
    <p>Weeks 4–7 are track-specific sprints. Each track has its own syllabus, deliverables, and support. You work in teams of three to four students. Each sprint produces a real, tested component that connects to the Knowledge Atlas infrastructure. Your methodology log documents the process: the decisions you made, the obstacles you overcame, and the evidence that justified your choices.</p>
    <p>Choosing a track is a serious commitment, but the choice reflects your interests and strengths. You have had two weeks to explore. If you have not decided by Week 3, this page and the track assignment pages will help you choose. The track signup process is straightforward: select a track, identify your teammates or indicate that you are willing to be grouped, and wait for formal team assignment. You can change tracks until the end of Week 3.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- ── Comparison Table ── -->
  <div class="section">
    <h2>Track Comparison</h2>
    <table class="comparison-table">
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th>Track</th>
          <th>Focus Area</th>
          <th>Tools You'll Use</th>
          <th>Key Deliverables</th>
          <th>Skills Developed</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        <tr>
          <td><strong>Track 1:<br/>Image Tagger</strong></td>
          <td>Evidence-based image annotation</td>
          <td>Python, JSON schemas, K-ATLAS API</td>
          <td>Annotation tool, tagged image dataset, validation report</td>
          <td>Data verification, pipeline architecture, schema design</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td><strong>Track 2:<br/>Article Finder</strong></td>
          <td>Literature retrieval pipeline</td>
          <td>Python, Google Scholar API, PubMed, SQL</td>
          <td>Query engine, deduplication system, 150+ citations</td>
          <td>Search methodology, database design, batch processing</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td><strong>Track 3:<br/>VR Production</strong></td>
          <td>3D environment design</td>
          <td>Unreal Engine / A-Frame, 3D modeling</td>
          <td>VR prototype, sensor logging, design specs</td>
          <td>3D design, experimental paradigm implementation, instrumentation</td>
        </tr>

    </table>
  </div>

  <!-- ── Detailed Track Cards ── -->
  <div class="section">
    <h2>Detailed Track Descriptions</h2>

    <div class="track-cards">
      <!-- Track 1 -->
      <div class="track-card track1">
        <h3>Track 1: Image Tagger</h3>
        <p><strong>What you'll build:</strong> A tool and workflow for annotating architectural photographs with evidence-backed psychological constructs. Your system will verify that each tag is supported by the K-ATLAS evidence base — no invention, only evidence-driven classification.</p>
        <div class="track-desc">
          <strong>Week-by-week:</strong><br/>
          Week 4: Design annotation schema and tag hierarchy. Build prototype tool.<br/>
          Week 5: Pilot annotation on 200 images. Refine schema based on results.<br/>
          Week 6: Full annotation run on 1,000 images. Validation and quality control.<br/>
          Week 7: Final deliverables, usability feedback, integration testing.
        </div>
        <div class="card-links">
          <a href="ka_tag_assignment.html" class="card-link card-link-primary">Full Assignment →</a>
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Track 2 -->
      <div class="track-card track2">
        <h3>Track 2: Article Finder</h3>
        <p><strong>What you'll build:</strong> A query engine and batch retrieval system that finds relevant peer-reviewed articles for K-ATLAS research questions. Your system will handle deduplication, verify schema compliance, and maintain database integrity under real-world search conditions.</p>
        <div class="track-desc">
          <strong>Week-by-week:</strong><br/>
          Week 4: Design query protocol. Build API connectors to Google Scholar and PubMed.<br/>
          Week 5: Implement deduplication and schema validation. Test on 50 example queries.<br/>
          Week 6: Scale to 130 K-ATLAS questions. Handle edge cases and failure modes.<br/>
          Week 7: Final retrieval of 150+ curated citations. Integration with main system.
        </div>
        <div class="card-links">
          <a href="ka_article_finder_assignment.html" class="card-link card-link-primary">Full Assignment →</a>
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Track 3 -->
      <div class="track-card track3">
        <h3>Track 3: VR Production</h3>
        <p><strong>What you'll build:</strong> Interactive 3D environments that visualize epistemological concepts and warrant structures. Your prototypes will run in Unreal Engine or A-Frame and include sensor logging so users can see how their exploration affects the evidence graph.</p>
        <div class="track-desc">
          <strong>Week-by-week:</strong><br/>
          Week 4: Learn engine, design environment spec, create initial 3D models.<br/>
          Week 5: Implement interactive warrant visualization and user navigation.<br/>
          Week 6: Add sensor logging and state persistence. Test interaction paradigm.<br/>
          Week 7: Polish, documentation, final demo, transition to fall continuity.
        </div>
        <div class="card-links">
          <a href="ka_vr_assignment.html" class="card-link card-link-primary">Full Assignment →</a>
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Track 4 -->
      <div class="track-card track4">
        <h3>Track 4: GUI Evaluation</h3>
        <p><strong>What you'll build:</strong> A web interface for researchers to explore the K-ATLAS evidence graph. Your interface will be tested against acceptance criteria you write, documented in a usability report, and accompanied by a spec wall showing the decision history.</p>
        <div class="track-desc">
          <strong>Week-by-week:</strong><br/>
          Week 4: Design acceptance criteria and user personas. Create wireframes and interaction spec.<br/>
          Week 5: Build prototype interface. Implement core search and navigation features.<br/>
          Week 6: User testing with 10–12 researchers. Document findings and iterate.<br/>
          Week 7: Final interface, usability report, spec wall, integration testing.
        </div>
        <div class="card-links">
          <a href="ka_gui_assignment.html" class="card-link card-link-primary">Full Assignment →</a>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- ── Signup Section ── -->
  <div class="section" id="signup">
    <h2>Sign Up for Your Track</h2>

    <div class="callout callout-teal">
      <div class="callout-label">Form Status</div>
      <p>The signup form will be activated during Thursday's seminar (Week 3, Day 5). You can browse all track details and prepare your choice now. Return here after the presentations to complete signup.</p>
    </div>

    <form style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="name">Your Name</label>
        <input type="text" id="name" name="name" placeholder="First and Last Name" disabled>
      </div>

      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="email">Email Address</label>
        <input type="email" id="email" name="email" placeholder="your.email@ucsd.edu" disabled>
      </div>

      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="track">Choose Your Track</label>
        <select id="track" name="track" disabled>
          <option value="">-- Select a track --</option>
          <option value="tagger">Track 1: Image Tagger</option>
          <option value="finder">Track 2: Article Finder</option>
          <option value="vr">Track 3: VR Production</option>
          <option value="gui">Track 4: GUI Evaluation</option>
        </select>
      </div>

      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="reason">Why this track? (Optional)</label>
        <textarea id="reason" name="reason" placeholder="Tell us what draws you to this track..." disabled></textarea>
      </div>

      <button type="submit" class="form-button" disabled>Submit Signup</button>
      <p class="signup-note">Form will be enabled during Week 3 seminar.</p>
    </form>

    <p style="margin-top: 1.5rem; font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--muted);">You can change tracks until the end of Week 3. After that, your team depends on you to stay committed.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- ── FAQ ── -->
  <div class="section">
    <h2>Frequently Asked Questions</h2>

    <div class="faq-item">
      <div class="faq-q">Can I switch tracks after signup?</div>
      <div class="faq-a">Yes, through the end of Week 3 (by Thursday of Week 3). After teams form and team contracts are finalized, switching is no longer possible because your teammates depend on you. If you are uncertain about your choice, use this week to explore thoroughly.</div>
    </div>

    <div class="faq-item">
      <div class="faq-q">What if I have no coding experience?</div>
      <div class="faq-a">Every track involves coding, but the specific skills vary. Track 1 (Image Tagger) and Track 2 (Article Finder) are Python-heavy. Track 3 (VR Production) focuses on 3D design and visual programming. Track 4 (GUI Evaluation) emphasizes frontend development and user testing. Choose based on which skill set interests you most and which gap you think is most important. Your teammates will likely have complementary strengths.</div>
    </div>

    <div class="faq-item">
      <div class="faq-q">Do I need VR hardware for Track 3?</div>
      <div class="faq-a">No. You will develop using Unreal Engine or A-Frame, both of which run on standard laptops and can be tested in desktop mode. VR headset support is a bonus feature for Week 8 and the fall continuation, not a requirement for this quarter's deliverables.</div>
    </div>

    <div class="faq-item">
      <div class="faq-q">What's the time commitment?</div>
      <div class="faq-a">Weeks 4–7 are intensive. Expect 12–15 hours per week during sprint weeks, with roughly 8 hours in class and 4–7 hours outside class for your track's work. The actual load depends on how efficiently your team coordinates. Teams that plan well and divide labor clearly tend to run lean. Teams that improvise spend more time debugging.</div>
    </div>

    <div class="faq-item">
      <div class="faq-q">What if I want to work alone?</div>
      <div class="faq-a">Tracks are team-based. The minimum team size is three students. If you do not have teammates in mind, indicate that on the signup form and you will be matched with other unmatched students from your chosen track.</div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- ── Navigation ── -->
  <div class="nav-links">
    <a href="ka_schedule.html" class="nav-back">← Back to Schedule</a>
    <a href="ka_student_setup.html" class="nav-back">Student Setup</a>
  </div>

</div>

</body>
</html>

<script>
window.KA_PAGE_FUNCTION = {
  pageId: 'ka_dashboard',
  title: 'Student Dashboard',
  audience: 'Students enrolled in COGS 160 [Cognitive Science 160 — Experimental Design in Human Factors] after login',
  purpose: 'The personal hub for a student contributor. Shows their progress on assigned tasks (image tagging quota, article evaluations, APA [American Psychological Association] bibliography entries, hypothesis submission), upcoming deadlines, and links to all contributor tools. In the live system this page is driven entirely by real database queries per student ID.',
  workflowPos: 'Immediately post-login for student users. The student returns here after completing each contributor task to see progress updated and discover what to do next.',
  notFor: 'Instructor-level views (see ka_approve.html), research queries, or browsing evidence. Should not show data from other students.',
  phase: 'Phase 3 — User Management (requires per-student DB queries and assignment tracking)',
  evalQuestions: [
    'Can a student immediately see what they should do today without reading any instructions?',
    'Are deadlines communicated with appropriate urgency (not alarmist, not invisible)?',
    'Is the progress bar system legible — does it show absolute numbers as well as percentages?',
    'Are links to contributor tools (Tag, Articles, Capture) prominent enough?',
    'Does the page distinguish clearly between completed, in-progress, and not-started assignments?'
  ]
};
</script>
<script src="../ka_page_function.js"></script>
<!-- ka_demo_wiring.js removed: live backend active -->
<script src="../ka_mode_switch.js"></script>

<script src="../ka_acronyms.js"></script>
<script>
(function() {
  function renderProgress(progress) {
    if (!progress) return;
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-progress-key]').forEach(function(row) {
      const key = row.getAttribute('data-progress-key');
      const item = progress[key];
      if (!item) return;
      const done = Number(item.done || 0);
      const target = Number(item.target || 0);
      const percent = target > 0 ? Math.min(100, (done / target) * 100) : 0;
      const bar = row.querySelector('.progress-bar');
      const text = row.querySelector('.progress-text');
      const link = row.querySelector('.progress-link');
      if (bar) bar.style.width = percent + '%';
      if (text) text.textContent = `${done}/${target}`;
      if (link && item.href) link.href = item.href;
    });
  }

  function renderActivity(items) {
    const wrap = document.getElementById('dashboard-activity-list');
    if (!wrap || !items || !items.length) return;
    wrap.innerHTML = items.map(function(item) {
      return `
        <div class="activity-item">
          <div class="activity-icon"></div>
          <div class="activity-content">
            <div class="activity-type">${item.type}</div>
            <div class="activity-date">${item.date}</div>
            <span class="activity-badge">${item.badge}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      `;
    }).join('');
  }

  function renderLeaderboard(items) {
    const tbody = document.querySelector('.leaderboard-table tbody');
    if (!tbody || !items || !items.length) return;
    tbody.innerHTML = items.map(function(item) {
      const yourRow = /you/i.test(item.name) ? ' class="leaderboard-your-row"' : '';
      return `
        <tr${yourRow}>
          <td class="leaderboard-rank">${item.rank}</td>
          <td class="leaderboard-name">${item.name}</td>
          <td>${item.count}</td>
        </tr>
      `;
    }).join('');
  }

  function coverageGoodish(fieldName, counter) {
    if (!counter) return 0;
    if (fieldName === 'abstract') {
      return Number(counter.good || 0) + Number(counter.provisional || 0);
    }
    if (['subject_count_total', 'sample_n', 'p_value', 'effect_size', 'main_conclusion'].includes(fieldName)) {
      return Number(counter.accepted || 0) + Number(counter.provisional || 0);
    }
    return Number(counter.good || 0);
  }

  function renderFieldCoverage(coverage) {
    const table = document.getElementById('dashboard-field-coverage-table');
    if (!table || !coverage || !coverage.article_type_counts) return;
    const tbody = table.querySelector('tbody');
    if (!tbody) return;
    const byType = coverage.by_article_type || {};
    const rows = Object.entries(coverage.article_type_counts)
      .sort(function(a, b) { return b[1] - a[1]; })
      .map(function(entry) {
        const articleType = entry[0];
        const total = Number(entry[1] || 0);
        const counters = byType[articleType] || {};
        function cell(fieldName) {
          const value = coverageGoodish(fieldName, counters[fieldName]);
          return `${value}/${total}`;
        }
        return `
          <tr>
            <td class="progress-label">${articleType.replace(/_/g, ' ')}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${total}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${cell('abstract')}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${cell('main_conclusion')}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${cell('subject_count_total')}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${cell('sample_n')}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${cell('p_value')}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${cell('effect_size')}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${cell('direction')}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${cell('stimulus_description')}</td>
            <td class="progress-text">${cell('methods_surface')}</td>
          </tr>
        `;
      });
    tbody.innerHTML = rows.join('');
  }

  async function initializeDashboardPage() {
    const payload = await window.KA_PAYLOADS.loadWithFallback('data/ka_payloads/dashboard.json', {});
    const jsonStatusPayload = await window.KA_PAYLOADS.loadWithFallback('data/ka_payloads/json_status.json', {});
    const layersPayload = await window.KA_PAYLOADS.loadWithFallback('data/ka_payloads/layers.json', {});
    const dashboard = payload.dashboard || {};
    const jsonSummary = jsonStatusPayload.summary || {};
    const layerMap = {};
    (layersPayload.layers || []).forEach(function(layer) {
      layerMap[layer.id] = layer;
    });
    const currentUser = window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE ? window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.currentUser() : null;
    const contributionStore = window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE ? window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.intakeSubmissions() : [];
    const myRows = currentUser && currentUser.id
      ? contributionStore.filter(function(row) { return row.userId === currentUser.id; })
      : [];
    if (dashboard.student_name) {
      document.getElementById('dashboard-user-name').textContent = dashboard.student_name;
      document.getElementById('dashboard-welcome-name').textContent = `Welcome back, ${dashboard.student_name.split(' ')[0]}`;
    }
    if (currentUser) {
      const fullName = [currentUser.firstName, currentUser.lastName].filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim();
      if (fullName) {
        document.getElementById('dashboard-user-name').textContent = fullName;
        document.getElementById('dashboard-welcome-name').textContent = `Welcome back, ${currentUser.firstName || fullName}`;
      }
      if (currentUser.email) {
        document.getElementById('dashboard-user-email').textContent = currentUser.email;
      }
    }
    if (dashboard.track) {
      document.getElementById('dashboard-track-badge').textContent = dashboard.track;
      document.getElementById('dashboard-week-label').innerHTML = `<strong>${dashboard.track}</strong> · ${dashboard.week_label || 'Current sprint'}`;
      document.getElementById('dashboard-track-title').textContent = `${dashboard.track}: Active Workstream`;
    }
    if (currentUser && currentUser.trackChoice1) {
      const trackLabel = currentUser.trackChoice1.replace('track', 'Track ');
      document.getElementById('dashboard-track-badge').textContent = trackLabel;
      document.getElementById('dashboard-week-label').innerHTML = `<strong>${trackLabel}</strong> · ${dashboard.week_label || 'Current sprint'}`;
      document.getElementById('dashboard-track-title').textContent = `${trackLabel}: Active Workstream`;
    }
    if (typeof dashboard.next_due_days !== 'undefined') {
      document.getElementById('dashboard-due-label').innerHTML = `Your next assignment is due in <strong>${dashboard.next_due_days} days</strong>.`;
    }
      document.getElementById('dashboard-progress-meta').textContent = 'Progress is sourced from rebuild payloads plus the workflow database snapshot, and will tighten further as live assignment tracking is wired.';
    document.getElementById('dashboard-track-copy').textContent = 'This dashboard is now pointed at rebuild-backed scientific data plus DB-backed workflow state, so progress and leaderboard areas can be replaced incrementally with live course state.';
    document.getElementById('dashboard-deadline-note').textContent = 'Deadline cards remain partly staged until the course tracker is wired to assignment records.';
    if (myRows.length) {
      dashboard.progress = dashboard.progress || {};
      dashboard.progress.apa_submissions = {
        done: myRows.filter(function(row) { return row.kind === 'citation'; }).length,
        target: 20,
        href: 'ka_article_propose.html'
      };
      dashboard.progress.pdfs_uploaded = {
        done: myRows.filter(function(row) { return row.kind !== 'citation'; }).length,
        target: 10,
        href: 'ka_article_propose.html'
      };
      dashboard.progress.articles_evaluated = {
        done: myRows.length,
        target: 15,
        href: 'ka_articles.html'
      };
      dashboard.recent_activity = myRows.slice(0, 5).map(function(row) {
        return {
          type: `${row.kind === 'citation' ? 'Citation' : 'PDF'} submitted: ${row.title}`,
          date: row.submissionId || 'Current session',
          badge: String(row.status || 'pending').toUpperCase()
        };
      });
      document.getElementById('dashboard-progress-meta').textContent = 'Progress is now sourced from the workflow snapshot plus your current-session overlay submissions.';
    }
    document.getElementById('dashboard-json-title-good').textContent = String(jsonSummary.title_good || 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-json-title-backlog').textContent = String((jsonSummary.title_provisional || 0) + (jsonSummary.title_missing_or_blocked || 0));
    document.getElementById('dashboard-json-abstract-good').textContent = String(jsonSummary.abstract_good || 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-json-subject-missing').textContent = String(jsonSummary.subject_count_missing || 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-json-sample-accepted').textContent = String(jsonSummary.sample_n_accepted || 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-json-sample-review').textContent = String(jsonSummary.sample_n_review_required || 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-json-p-accepted').textContent = String(jsonSummary.p_value_accepted || 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-json-conclusion-accepted').textContent = String(jsonSummary.main_conclusion_accepted || 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-json-effect-accepted').textContent = String(jsonSummary.effect_size_accepted || 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-layer-argumentation').textContent = String(layerMap.argumentation ? layerMap.argumentation.primary_metric : 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-layer-annotations').textContent = String(layerMap.annotations ? layerMap.annotations.primary_metric : 0);
    document.getElementById('dashboard-layer-interpretation').textContent = String(layerMap.interpretation ? layerMap.interpretation.primary_metric : 0);
    if (jsonSummary.papers_total) {
      document.getElementById('dashboard-json-status-copy').textContent = `Current payload coverage across ${jsonSummary.papers_total} papers. Provisional and missing fields stay visible here so we can keep repairing the JSONs while the site is already reviewable.`;
    }
    renderFieldCoverage(dashboard.field_coverage_by_article_type);
    renderProgress(dashboard.progress);
    renderActivity(dashboard.recent_activity);
    renderLeaderboard(dashboard.leaderboard);
  }

  window.KA_SHELL.initShell({
    navContainerSelector: 'nav ul',
    modeSelectId: 'dashboard-mode-select',
    modePillId: 'dashboard-mode-pill',
    defaultMode: 'contributor'
  });
  initializeDashboardPage();
})();
</script>

<script>
// JWT-aware research question widget
// Calls GET /api/assignments on ka_auth_server.py (port 8765) if a token is present.
// Gracefully no-ops if server is unreachable or user is not authenticated.
(function() {
  const KA_AUTH_API = window.__KA_CONFIG__?.apiBase ?? '';
  const token = localStorage.getItem('ka_access_token');
  if (!token) return;  // not logged in via JWT — skip silently

  fetch(KA_AUTH_API + '/api/assignments', {
    headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token }
  })
  .then(function(res) { return res.ok ? res.json() : Promise.reject(res.status); })
  .then(function(data) {
    const card = document.getElementById('rq-assignment-card');
    if (!card) return;
    card.style.display = '';
    if (data && data.question_id) {
      document.getElementById('rq-id').textContent = data.question_id;
      document.getElementById('rq-title').textContent = data.title || '';
      document.getElementById('rq-desc').textContent = data.description || '';
    } else {
      document.getElementById('rq-assignment-body').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('rq-unassigned').style.display = '';
    }
  })
  .catch(function() {
    // Auth server not running — do not show the card at all
  });
})();
</script>

    <script src="../data/ka_payloads/workflow.js"></script>
    <script src="../ka_workflow_store.js"></script>
    <script>
        // ── ROW EXPAND ──
        function expandRow(rowElement) {
            const nextRow = rowElement.nextElementSibling;
            if (nextRow && nextRow.classList.contains('detail-panel')) {
                nextRow.classList.toggle('expanded');
                rowElement.classList.toggle('expanded');
            }
        }

        let _pendingApprovalName = '';
        let _pendingApprovalId = '';
        let _pendingRejectName   = '';
        let _pendingRejectId   = '';

        function workflowStore() {
            return window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE;
        }

        function trackLabelFromCode(code) {
            const labels = {
                track1: 'Track 1 — Image Tagging',
                track2: 'Track 2 — Article Finding',
                track3: 'Track 3 — VR Production',
                track4: 'Track 4 — GUI Evaluation & Experiment Design'
            };
            return labels[code] || code || '—';
        }

        function allRegistrationRows() {
            return workflowStore() ? workflowStore().allUsers() : [];
        }

        function registrationById(userId) {
            return allRegistrationRows().find(function(row) { return row.id === userId; }) || null;
        }

        function renderApprovalQueue() {
            const rows = allRegistrationRows();
            const pending = rows.filter(function(row) { return String(row.status || 'pending') === 'pending'; });
            const approved = rows.filter(function(row) { return row.status === 'approved'; });
            const rejected = rows.filter(function(row) { return row.status === 'rejected'; });

            const badge = document.getElementById('pending-request-badge');
            if (badge) badge.textContent = String(pending.length);

            const body = document.getElementById('approval-table-body');
            if (body) {
                body.innerHTML = pending.length ? pending.map(function(row) {
                    const fullName = [row.firstName, row.lastName].filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim() || row.email || row.id;
                    const institution = row.institution || 'Institution not provided';
                    const submitted = row.timestamp ? new Date(row.timestamp).toLocaleDateString() : '—';
                    return `
                        <tr onclick="expandRow(this)">
                            <td class="name-cell">${fullName}</td>
                            <td>${institution}</td>
                            <td><span class="track-badge">${trackLabelFromCode(row.trackChoice1)}</span></td>
                            <td><span class="track-badge">${trackLabelFromCode(row.trackChoice2)}</span></td>
                            <td><span class="skills-truncate">${(row.department || row.role || 'Profile pending detail').slice(0, 80)}</span></td>
                            <td>${submitted}</td>
                            <td>
                                <div class="action-buttons">
                                    <button class="btn-small btn-approve-t1" data-user-id="${row.id}" data-track="${trackLabelFromCode(row.trackChoice1)}">Approve T1</button>
                                    <button class="btn-small btn-approve-t2" data-user-id="${row.id}" data-track="${trackLabelFromCode(row.trackChoice2 || row.trackChoice1)}">Approve T2</button>
                                    <button class="btn-small btn-reject" data-user-id="${row.id}">Reject</button>
                                </div>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                        <tr class="detail-panel">
                            <td colspan="7">
                                <div class="detail-grid">
                                    <div class="detail-field">
                                        <div class="detail-label">Academic Profile</div>
                                        <div class="detail-value">${row.role || 'Not specified'} · ${row.department || 'Department not specified'}</div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="detail-field">
                                        <div class="detail-label">Email</div>
                                        <div class="detail-value">${row.email || 'Not provided'}</div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="detail-field">
                                        <div class="detail-label">Institution</div>
                                        <div class="detail-value">${institution}</div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="detail-field">
                                        <div class="detail-label">Workflow status</div>
                                        <div class="detail-value">Pending approval · ${row.userType || 'user type unspecified'}</div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                    `;
                }).join('') : `
                    <tr>
                        <td colspan="7" style="padding:20px;color:#6D645A;">No pending registrations are stored in the current workflow state.</td>
                    </tr>
                `;
            }

            const approvedList = document.getElementById('approved-requests-list');
            if (approvedList) {
                approvedList.innerHTML = approved.length ? approved.map(function(row) {
                    const fullName = [row.firstName, row.lastName].filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim() || row.email || row.id;
                    return `<div class="capacity-text"><strong>${fullName}</strong> · ${row.approvedTrack || trackLabelFromCode(row.trackChoice1)} · ${row.email || 'email missing'}</div>`;
                }).join('') : '<div class="capacity-text">No approved registrations are stored yet.</div>';
            }

            const rejectedList = document.getElementById('rejected-requests-list');
            if (rejectedList) {
                rejectedList.innerHTML = rejected.length ? rejected.map(function(row) {
                    const fullName = [row.firstName, row.lastName].filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim() || row.email || row.id;
                    return `<div class="capacity-text"><strong>${fullName}</strong> · ${row.rejectionReason || 'No rejection reason recorded.'}</div>`;
                }).join('') : '<div class="capacity-text">No rejected registrations are stored yet.</div>';
            }

            const allUsersList = document.getElementById('all-users-list');
            if (allUsersList) {
                allUsersList.innerHTML = rows.length ? rows.map(function(row) {
                    const fullName = [row.firstName, row.lastName].filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim() || row.email || row.id;
                    return `<div class="capacity-text"><strong>${fullName}</strong> · ${row.status || 'pending'} · ${trackLabelFromCode(row.approvedTrack || row.trackChoice1)}</div>`;
                }).join('') : '<div class="capacity-text">No registrations are stored in the current workflow state.</div>';
            }

            const rosterList = document.getElementById('track-roster-list');
            if (rosterList) {
                const roster = workflowStore() ? workflowStore().trackRoster() : {};
                const labels = Object.keys(roster);
                rosterList.innerHTML = labels.length ? labels.map(function(label) {
                    return `<div class="capacity-text"><strong>${label}</strong> · ${(roster[label] || []).length} approved contributor(s)</div>`;
                }).join('') : '<div class="capacity-text">Track roster remains empty until approvals are recorded.</div>';
            }

            const capacityGrid = document.getElementById('track-capacity-grid');
            if (capacityGrid && workflowStore()) {
                capacityGrid.innerHTML = workflowStore().trackCapacity().map(function(row) {
                    return `
                        <div class="capacity-card">
                            <div class="capacity-card-title">${row.label}</div>
                            <div class="capacity-bar">
                                <div class="capacity-fill" style="width: ${row.pct}%;"></div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="capacity-text">${row.approved} approved / ${row.target || 'TBD'} target</div>
                        </div>
                    `;
                }).join('');
            }

            document.querySelectorAll('.btn-small').forEach(function(btn) {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    const userId = this.getAttribute('data-user-id');
                    const row = registrationById(userId);
                    const studentName = row ? ([row.firstName, row.lastName].filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim() || row.email || row.id) : 'Unknown applicant';
                    if (this.classList.contains('btn-reject')) {
                        openRejectModal(studentName, userId);
                    } else {
                        openApproveModal(studentName, userId, this.getAttribute('data-track'));
                    }
                });
            });
        }

        // ── APPROVE MODAL ──
        function openApproveModal(name, userId, preferredTrack) {
            _pendingApprovalName = name;
            _pendingApprovalId = userId || '';
            const row = registrationById(userId) || {};
            const d = {
                inst: row.institution || '—',
                email: row.email || '—',
                date: row.timestamp ? new Date(row.timestamp).toLocaleDateString() : '—',
                t1: preferredTrack || trackLabelFromCode(row.trackChoice1),
                t2: trackLabelFromCode(row.trackChoice2)
            };
            document.getElementById('approve-name').textContent  = name;
            document.getElementById('approve-inst').textContent  = d.inst;
            document.getElementById('approve-email').textContent = d.email;
            document.getElementById('approve-date').textContent  = d.date;
            document.getElementById('approve-t1').textContent    = d.t1;
            document.getElementById('approve-t2').textContent    = d.t2;
            document.getElementById('approve-overlay').classList.add('open');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        }
        function closeApproveModal(e) {
            if (e && e.target !== document.getElementById('approve-overlay')) return;
            document.getElementById('approve-overlay').classList.remove('open');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }
        function toggleApproveTrack(el) {
            document.querySelectorAll('#approve-track-btns .ar-track-badge')
                .forEach(b => b.classList.add('inactive'));
            el.classList.remove('inactive');
        }
        function confirmApprove() {
            const trackEl = document.querySelector('#approve-track-btns .ar-track-badge:not(.inactive)');
            const track = trackEl ? trackEl.textContent : 'Primary Track';
            if (workflowStore() && _pendingApprovalId) {
                workflowStore().approveRegistration(_pendingApprovalId, track);
                renderApprovalQueue();
            }
            closeApproveModal();
            showARToast(`✅ ${_pendingApprovalName} approved for ${track}`, 'approve');
        }

        // ── REJECT MODAL ──
        function openRejectModal(name, userId) {
            _pendingRejectName = name;
            _pendingRejectId = userId || '';
            document.getElementById('reject-name').textContent = name;
            const row = registrationById(userId) || {};
            const d = { inst: row.institution || '—' };
            document.getElementById('reject-inst').textContent = d.inst;
            document.getElementById('reject-note').value = '';
            ['rr-capacity','rr-skills','rr-incomplete','rr-timing'].forEach(id => {
                const el = document.getElementById(id);
                if (el) el.checked = false;
            });
            document.getElementById('reject-overlay').classList.add('open');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        }
        function closeRejectModal(e) {
            if (e && e.target !== document.getElementById('reject-overlay')) return;
            document.getElementById('reject-overlay').classList.remove('open');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }
        function confirmReject() {
            const reason = document.getElementById('reject-note').value.trim();
            if (workflowStore() && _pendingRejectId) {
                workflowStore().rejectRegistration(_pendingRejectId, reason);
                renderApprovalQueue();
            }
            closeRejectModal();
            showARToast(`Decline notice sent to ${_pendingRejectName}`, 'reject');
        }

        function showARToast(msg, type) {
            const t = document.getElementById('ar-toast');
            t.textContent = msg;
            t.className = `ar-toast ${type}`;
            t.style.display = 'block';
            clearTimeout(t._timer);
            t._timer = setTimeout(() => { t.style.display = 'none'; }, 3200);
        }

        renderApprovalQueue();

        document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
            if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                document.getElementById('approve-overlay').classList.remove('open');
                document.getElementById('reject-overlay').classList.remove('open');
                document.body.style.overflow = '';
            }
        });
    </script>

<script>

<div class="page-hero">
  <div class="hero-eyebrow">COGS 160 · Spring 2026 · 10 Weeks</div>
  <h1 class="hero-title">Course Schedule</h1>
  <p class="hero-sub">What happens each week, what is due by Thursday, and which pages on this site you need to use. Click any week to expand it.</p>
  <div class="hero-pills">
    <span class="hero-pill">Weeks 1–2 · Everyone builds the archive</span>
    <span class="hero-pill">Weeks 3–7 · Track work</span>
    <span class="hero-pill">Weeks 8–10 · Debugging the Fall site</span>
  </div>
</div>

<div class="container">

  <!-- ── PHASE 1 BANNER ── -->
  <div class="phase-banner phase-all">
    <div class="phase-banner-icon">📚</div>
    <div>
      <div class="phase-banner-title">Phase 1 — Weeks 1–2 · Whole class, same task</div>
      <div class="phase-banner-desc">
        Before any track work begins, every student does the same thing: explore the Knowledge Atlas site, learn how to find and evaluate scientific articles using AI-assisted search, and submit PDFs to the shared archive. This builds the raw material all four tracks will draw on. You also begin noticing usability issues with the site — that observation work is already Track 4 territory and counts.
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- WEEK 1 -->
  <div class="week-card phase-all-card">
    <div class="week-header" onclick="toggleWeek('w1')">
      <div class="week-num">
        <div class="week-num-label">Week</div>
        <div class="week-num-value">1</div>
      </div>
      <div class="week-summary">
        <div class="week-title">Orientation · Meeting the system · First articles</div>
        <div class="week-tagline">Day 1: Get oriented and meet the system. Day 2: Find 20 articles using AI search tools.</div>
        <div class="week-badges">
          <span class="badge badge-teal">Everyone</span>
          <span class="badge badge-amber">Due Mon Wk 2: 20 PDFs submitted</span>
          <a href="week1_agenda.html" class="week-agenda-link" onclick="event.stopPropagation()">View Full Agenda →</a>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="week-expand" id="w1-arrow">＋</div>
    </div>
    <div class="week-body" id="w1">

      <div class="day-row">
        <div class="day-label">Tuesday<span>Day 1</span></div>
        <div class="day-content">
          <div class="session-title">Orientation — What is Knowledge Atlas and why are we building it?</div>
          <div class="session-desc">
            <p>Prof Kirsh introduces the course, the Knowledge Atlas system, and the four contributor tracks. The session is primarily explanatory — you are not expected to have done anything before arriving.</p>
          </div>
          <ul class="task-list">
            <li>Register on the site if you have not already — use the Register button on the homepage</li>
            <li>Look around the site: homepage, topics, evidence, sensors, sitemap</li>
            <li>Identify which of the four tracks you want to join — you declared a preference at registration, but this week you can still change your mind</li>
            <li>Read the short "About this page" section (bottom-right badge) on any page you visit to understand what it does</li>
          </ul>
          <div class="page-links">
            <a href="../ka_home.html" class="page-link">Home</a>
            <a href="../ka_register.html" class="page-link">Register</a>
            <a href="../ka_topics.html" class="page-link">Topics</a>
            <a href="../ka_sitemap.html" class="page-link">Site Map</a>
            <a href="../ka_ai_methodology.html" class="page-link">AI Methodology</a>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="day-row">
        <div class="day-label">Thursday<span>Day 2</span></div>
        <div class="day-content">
          <div class="session-title">AI-Assisted Article Finding — Lab session</div>
          <div class="session-desc">
            <p>Prof Kirsh is away. A lab member will be present to assist. The goal is hands-on: find and submit at least 20 PDFs of relevant scientific articles by Monday of Week 2. Use Google Scholar AI for your searches.</p>
            <p>Start by visiting the Topics page to identify which research area you want to search in. Then use the Question Maker to turn a topic into search-ready queries (the point is to move beyond simple Boolean strings toward richer, semantically-grounded queries).</p>
          </div>
          <ul class="task-list">
            <li>Visit Topics — pick one or two research areas that interest you</li>
            <li>Use the Question Maker to generate search queries that go beyond keyword Boolean logic</li>
            <li>Search using: <strong>Google Scholar AI</strong> <span style="color:#B0A090; text-decoration:line-through;">Elicit</span> <span style="color:#B0A090; text-decoration:line-through;">OpenAlex</span> <span style="color:#B0A090; text-decoration:line-through;">Consensus</span> <span style="color:#B0A090; text-decoration:line-through;">Scholar GPT</span></li>
            <li>Download PDFs for any article that looks relevant and well-cited</li>
            <li>Submit 20 PDFs to the article archive by Monday of Week 2</li>
            <li>Start a plain-text note of any site friction you encountered — confusing labels, missing links, anything that slowed you down</li>
          </ul>
          <div class="deliverable-box">
            <div class="deliverable-box-label">Due Monday of Week 2</div>
            <p>20 PDFs submitted to the Knowledge Atlas article archive via the Article Propose page. These contribute directly to the shared evidence base all tracks will use.</p>
          </div>
          <div class="page-links">
            <a href="../ka_topics.html" class="page-link">Topics</a>
            <a href="../ka_question_maker.html" class="page-link">Question Maker</a>
            <a href="../ka_article_search.html" class="page-link">Article Search</a>
            <a href="../ka_article_propose.html" class="page-link">Submit Articles</a>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

    </div>
  </div><!-- /week 1 -->

  <!-- WEEK 2 -->
  <div class="week-card phase-all-card">
    <div class="week-header" onclick="toggleWeek('w2')">
      <div class="week-num">
        <div class="week-num-label">Week</div>
        <div class="week-num-value">2</div>
      </div>
      <div class="week-summary">
        <div class="week-title">AI-Directed Programming · Live Demo · Your First Build</div>
        <div class="week-tagline">Watch Prof Kirsh demo the 7-step method live, then build a real component on the KA codebase using AI.</div>
        <div class="week-badges">
          <span class="badge badge-teal">Everyone</span>
          <a href="week2_agenda.html" class="week-agenda-link" onclick="event.stopPropagation()">View Full Agenda →</a>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="week-expand" id="w2-arrow">＋</div>
    </div>
    <div class="week-body" id="w2">

      <div class="day-row">
        <div class="day-label">Tuesday<span>Day 3</span></div>
        <div class="day-content">
          <div class="session-title">Brief Overview of Current System</div>
          <div class="session-desc">
            <p>We'll look at the high level structure of the system and what it is supposed to accomplish.</p>
          </div>
          <div class="page-links">
            <a href="week2_agenda.html" class="page-link">Week 2 Agenda</a>
          </div>
          <div class="session-title">Live Demo — AI-Directed Development in Action</div>
          <div class="session-desc">
            <p>Prof Kirsh demos the full 7-step method live: convene a panel, write a spec, define acceptance tests, implement with AI, verify, diagnose failures, and iterate. The demo task is Exercise 0 (Mechanism Pathway Tracer) — building a D3.js visualization that traces causal chains through the evidence network.</p>
            <p>Watch closely. Thursday you do the same thing yourself.</p>
          </div>
          <ul class="task-list">
            <li>Watch the live demo — take notes on where the spec did the intellectual work vs. where the AI did</li>
            <li>Notice how the panel surfaces requirements the developer wouldn't have thought of</li>
            <li>Notice what fails and how the diagnosis traces back to the spec, not the code</li>
            <li>Read your assigned exercise beforehand so you can follow along with understanding</li>
          </ul>
          <div class="page-links">
            <a href="week2_exercises.html" class="page-link" style="background:#E8872A;color:#fff;font-weight:700">Programming Exercises →</a>
            <a href="demo_pdf_relevance_filter.html" class="page-link">Demo: PDF Relevance Filter</a>
            <a href="week2_agenda.html" class="page-link">Live Demo</a>
            <a href="ka_technical_setup.html" class="page-link">Technical Setup</a>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="day-row">
        <div class="day-label">Thursday<span>Day 4</span></div>
        <div class="day-content">
          <div class="session-title">Your First AI-Directed Build</div>
          <div class="session-desc">
            <p>Now it's your turn. Each team is assigned one programming exercise — a real engineering task on the Knowledge Atlas codebase. You will use the same 7-step method Prof Kirsh demonstrated on Tuesday. The AI supplies the domain knowledge (via the panel and the context file). You supply the method.</p>
            <p>Start by loading your context file into the AI. Then ask the AI to explain the task back to you. Only then convene the panel.</p>
          </div>
          <ul class="task-list">
            <li><strong>Step 0:</strong> Paste your exercise's context file into the AI — this gives it the data schemas and file locations</li>
            <li><strong>Step 0.5:</strong> Ask the AI to explain what the task is about — correct any misunderstandings before proceeding</li>
            <li><strong>Steps 1–3:</strong> Convene panel, write spec, define acceptance tests — all before any code</li>
            <li><strong>Steps 4–7:</strong> Implement, verify, diagnose failures, iterate</li>
          </ul>
          <div class="deliverable-box">
            <div class="deliverable-box-label">Due by end of Thursday</div>
            <p>Submit a single document with: panel transcript, spec, all prompts (including failures), AI output, verification results, and two-paragraph reflection.</p>
          </div>
          <div class="page-links">
            <a href="week2_exercises.html" class="page-link" style="background:#E8872A;color:#fff;font-weight:700">Programming Exercises →</a>
            <a href="context/" class="page-link">Context Files</a>
            <a href="../ka_evidence.html" class="page-link">Evidence Explorer</a>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

    </div>
  </div><!-- /week 2 -->

  <div class="phase-banner phase-track">
    <div class="phase-banner-icon">🔧</div>
    <div>
      <div class="phase-banner-title">Phase 2 — Weeks 3–7 · Track-specific production work</div>
      <div class="phase-banner-desc">
        In Week 3 each team decides how they will divide labor and collaborate. From Week 3 through Week 7, work is track-specific: Track 1 builds the image-tagging pipeline, Track 2 scales the article archive and evaluates the intake pipeline, Track 3 produces VR research environments, and Track 4 conducts systematic GUI evaluation. Detailed deliverables and grading criteria for each week will be posted here as the quarter progresses.
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

            <li>Each person confirms their local environment works (git, Python, student DB copy)</li>

  <!-- ── PHASE 3 BANNER ── -->
  <div class="section-divider">
    <div class="divider-line"></div>
    <div class="divider-text">Phase 3 — Fall Site Debugging</div>
    <div class="divider-line"></div>
  </div>

  <div class="phase-banner phase-debug">
    <div class="phase-banner-icon">🔬</div>
    <div>
      <div class="phase-banner-title">Phase 3 — Weeks 8–10 · Debugging the Fall COGS 160 site</div>
      <div class="phase-banner-desc">
        The last three weeks shift from building to testing. Each team is assigned a section of the <strong>Designing_Experiments</strong> repository — the Fall COGS 160 experiment-making site being developed in parallel. Teams fork the repo, audit their section by simulating a naïve student walkthrough, fix every resolvable issue, write formal success conditions for each page function, and open a Pull Request with a hand-off report. The goal is a site that a new cohort of Fall students can actually use without instructor hand-holding. Sensor integration and adaptive psych instrument work (Q-sort, IAT) are available as alternatives for interested students.
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- WEEK 8 -->
  <div class="week-card phase-debug-card">
    <div class="week-header" onclick="toggleWeek('w8')">

        <div class="week-tagline">Each team receives a section of the Fall site. Begin simulating a student's first day.</div>

        <div class="day-label">Tuesday<span>Day 15</span></div>
        <div class="day-content">
          <div class="session-title">Site Assignment and Kickoff</div>
          <div class="session-desc"><p>Each team is assigned a section of the Fall COGS 160 experiment-making site. The instructor explains the overall architecture of that site and what it is supposed to do when finished.</p></div>
          <ul class="task-list blue">
            <li>Receive your team's site section assignment</li>
            <li>Read the existing code and identify what each page is intended to do</li>
            <li>Draft a list of the functions in your section that need success conditions written</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="day-row">
        <div class="day-label">Thursday<span>Day 16</span></div>
        <div class="day-content">
          <div class="session-title">First Student Simulation Walkthrough</div>
          <div class="session-desc"><p>Each person simulates the experience of a Fall student: start at the track overview page for your assigned section of Designing_Experiments and attempt to complete every stated task without outside help. Log every broken link, missing file, unclear instruction, and non-functional interactive element using the structured observation format.</p></div>
          <ul class="task-list blue">
            <li>Create your audit folder: <code>docs/phase3_audit/section_X/</code> — commit to your Phase 3 branch</li>
            <li>Run the end-to-end walkthrough; log at minimum 10 observations with severity ratings</li>
            <li>Write a one-paragraph README.md for your section</li>
            <li><strong>Due by end of class:</strong> push <code>walkthrough_log.md</code> and <code>README.md</code> to your branch</li>
          </ul>
          <div class="page-links"><a href="../Designing_Experiments/docs/student_tracks/phase3_wk08.html" style="color:var(--blue,#2A5FA0);font-weight:600">→ Full Week 8 assignment page (Designing_Experiments)</a></div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div><!-- /week 8 -->

  <!-- WEEK 9 -->
  <div class="week-card phase-debug-card">
    <div class="week-header" onclick="toggleWeek('w9')">

        <div class="week-title">Bug fixing · Success conditions · Sensor and psych test work</div>
        <div class="week-tagline">Fix the bugs you found. Write success conditions. Optional: sensor hookup and psych instrument work.</div>

    <div class="week-body" id="w9">
      <div class="day-row">
        <div class="day-label">Both days</div>
        <div class="day-content">
          <div class="session-desc"><p>Primary work: fix the issues found in Week 8 walkthroughs and write formal success conditions for each function in your assigned section. A success condition is a precise statement of what the function must do, what constitutes a correct output, and what a failure looks like.</p></div>
          <ul class="task-list blue">
            <li>Fix bugs identified in Week 8 walkthroughs — commit fixes to a debugging branch</li>
            <li>Write success conditions for each code function in your section (<code>success_conditions.md</code>)</li>
            <li>Optional: work with the instructor on sensor hookup for physiological stress measurement</li>
            <li>Optional: help design or implement adaptive preference tests, Q-sort instruments, or IATs for the Fall site</li>
          </ul>
          <ul class="task-list blue">
            <li>Triage your walkthrough log: mark each issue as RESOLVED, OPEN (with GitHub issue link), NOT-IN-SCOPE, or NEEDS-DECISION</li>
            <li>Fix all BLOCKING and MAJOR issues within your competence; commit each fix with a clear message</li>
            <li>Write at least one success condition per page in your section in <code>success_conditions.md</code></li>
            <li><strong>Due by end of Thursday:</strong> fixes committed, <code>success_conditions.md</code> and updated <code>walkthrough_log.md</code> pushed</li>
          </ul>
          <div class="info-box"><p><strong>Sensor and psych test track</strong> — students interested in the sensor hookup (wearable physiological measurement) or in building adaptive psychological instruments (Q-sort, implicit association tests, adaptive preference surveys) should speak with Prof Kirsh in Week 8 to confirm participation. This is an alternative to the site-debugging work, not additional to it.</p></div>
          <div class="page-links"><a href="../Designing_Experiments/docs/student_tracks/phase3_wk09.html" style="color:var(--blue,#2A5FA0);font-weight:600">→ Full Week 9 assignment page (Designing_Experiments)</a></div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div><!-- /week 9 -->

  <!-- WEEK 10 -->
  <div class="week-card phase-debug-card">
    <div class="week-header" onclick="toggleWeek('w10')">
      <div class="week-num"><div class="week-num-label">Week</div><div class="week-num-value">10</div></div>
      <div class="week-summary">
        <div class="week-title">Final walkthroughs · Hand-off report · Quarter review</div>
        <div class="week-tagline">Each team produces a final site-section report and presents findings.</div>
        <div class="week-badges"><span class="badge badge-blue">All teams</span><span class="badge badge-gray">Final deliverables to be posted</span></div>
      </div>
      <div class="week-expand" id="w10-arrow">＋</div>
    </div>
    <div class="week-body" id="w10">
      <div class="day-row">
        <div class="day-label">Tuesday<span>Day 19</span></div>
        <div class="day-content">
          <div class="session-title">Second Student Simulation Walkthrough</div>
          <div class="session-desc"><p>Repeat the Week 8 simulation on the now-partially-debugged site. How far does a naïve student get this time? What is still broken? This comparison — Week 8 state vs. Week 10 state — is part of the final deliverable.</p></div>
          <ul class="task-list blue">
            <li>Complete the end-to-end student simulation walkthrough on your section</li>
            <li>Document progress: what works now that did not in Week 8?</li>
            <li>List remaining open issues with severity ratings (blocking / major / minor)</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="day-row">
        <div class="day-label">Thursday<span>Day 20</span></div>
        <div class="day-content">
          <div class="session-title">Final Presentations and Hand-Off</div>
          <div class="session-desc"><p>Each team presents their section to the class (5–8 minutes): what was assigned, what they found, what they fixed, what remains open, and their success conditions. The goal is a hand-off document that the Fall instructor can use to continue development over the summer.</p></div>
          <ul class="task-list blue">
            <li>Re-run the simulation; produce <code>re_walkthrough_log.md</code> with a W8-vs-W10 comparison table</li>
            <li>Write <code>HANDOFF_REPORT.md</code>: section overview, state table, fixes made, open issues, success conditions, recommendations</li>
            <li>Open a Pull Request to Tag-UCSD/Designing_Experiments with your full audit folder and any fixed pages</li>
          </ul>
          <div class="page-links"><a href="../Designing_Experiments/docs/student_tracks/phase3_wk10.html" style="color:var(--blue,#2A5FA0);font-weight:600">→ Full Week 10 assignment page (Designing_Experiments)</a></div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div><!-- /week 10 -->

  <!-- GRADING NOTICE -->
  <div class="grading-notice">
    <h3>Grading</h3>
    <p>
      Detailed grading rubrics for the track work (Weeks 3–7) and the Fall site debugging (Weeks 8–10) will be posted on this page before those phases begin. The Week 1–2 article-finding work is assessed on completion (20 PDFs submitted by Monday of Week 2; continued submissions through Week 2). Usability notes are assessed on specificity — a generic comment such as "the site was confusing" does not count; a note such as "the Article Propose page does not explain whether uploaded PDFs replace a DOI entry or supplement it" does.
    </p>
  </div>

<script>
function toggleWeek(id) {
  const body = document.getElementById(id);
  const arrow = document.getElementById(id + '-arrow');
  const isOpen = body.classList.contains('open');
  body.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);
  arrow.textContent = isOpen ? '＋' : '－';
}

// Open week 1 by default
toggleWeek('w1');
</script>

// Class intro CTA — injected via JS to avoid HTML nesting issues
// Uses window.onload to ensure all DOM parsing is complete
window.addEventListener('load', function() {
  var footer = document.querySelector('footer.ka-page-footer');
  if (footer && !document.getElementById('class-intro-cta')) {
    var cta = document.createElement('div');
    cta.id = 'class-intro-cta';
    cta.style.cssText = 'text-align:center; padding:40px 20px 20px;';
    cta.innerHTML = '<a href="../ka_ai_methodology.html" style="display:inline-block; background:#E8872A; color:#fff; font-size:1.1rem; font-weight:700; padding:14px 36px; border-radius:8px; text-decoration:none; letter-spacing:0.3px; box-shadow:0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.15);">Next: AI Method &amp; Its Big Bugs →</a>';
    footer.parentNode.insertBefore(cta, footer);
  }
});
</script>

      <ol style="margin:0;padding-left:1.6rem;font-size:0.92rem;line-height:1.7;">
        <li style="margin-bottom:0.4rem;"><strong>Upload ten APA citations</strong> for EXPERIMENT ARTICLES — either one at a time copied into the text box, or upload a file with all 10.</li>
        <li style="margin-bottom:0.4rem;"><strong>Upload the PDFs</strong> that correspond to those citations.</li>
        <li style="margin-bottom:0.8rem;"><strong>We will verify</strong> that they are articles about experiments (not theory or meta-reviews) and that they are on the topic we assigned you.</li>
      </ol>
      <p style="font-size:0.92rem;line-height:1.7;margin:0.8rem 0 0;border-top:2px solid var(--border);padding-top:0.8rem;">Then:</p>
      <ol style="margin:0.8rem 0 0;padding-left:1.6rem;font-size:0.92rem;line-height:1.7;">
        <li><strong>Create a question</strong> for Google AI Scholar on one of our CNFA Topics and repeat the same APA + PDF upload process — but this time you can upload the 10 articles you think are the best, regardless of article type.</li>
      </ol>
    </div>

<script>
function toggleAccordion(header) {
  var body = header.nextElementSibling;
  var chevron = header.querySelector('.chevron');
  if (body.classList.contains('open')) {
    body.classList.remove('open');
    chevron.textContent = '▼';
  } else {
    body.classList.add('open');
    chevron.textContent = '▲';
  }
}

function switchTab(event, tabId) {
  // Hide all tab content
  var contents = event.target.parentElement.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.tab-content');
  contents.forEach(function(c) { c.classList.remove('active'); });

  // Remove active class from all buttons
  var buttons = event.target.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.tab-button');
  buttons.forEach(function(b) { b.classList.remove('active'); });

  // Show selected tab and mark button active
  document.getElementById(tabId).classList.add('active');
  event.target.classList.add('active');
}
</script>

<script>
async function joinTrack(trackId) {
  const KA_AUTH_API = window.__KA_CONFIG__?.apiBase ?? '';
  const token = localStorage.getItem('ka_access_token');
  const btn = document.getElementById('join-track-btn');
  const msg = document.getElementById('join-track-msg');
  if (!token) {
    msg.style.display = 'block';
    msg.style.background = '#fff3cd'; msg.style.color = '#856404';
    msg.textContent = 'Please sign in first to join a track.';
    return;
  }
  btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'Joining…';
  try {
    const res = await fetch(KA_AUTH_API + '/auth/update-track', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
      body: JSON.stringify({ track: trackId })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (res.ok) {
      msg.style.display = 'block';
      msg.style.background = '#d4edda'; msg.style.color = '#155724';
      msg.innerHTML = '&#10003; ' + data.message + '<br><small>This is now shown on your profile. You can change tracks later if needed.</small>';
      btn.textContent = '&#10003; Joined!'; btn.style.background = '#27ae60';
      // Update localStorage so profile shows the track
      try {
        const u = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ka_current_user') || '{}');
        u.track = trackId; localStorage.setItem('ka_current_user', JSON.stringify(u));
      } catch(e) {}
    } else {
      msg.style.display = 'block';
      msg.style.background = '#f8d7da'; msg.style.color = '#721c24';
      msg.textContent = data.detail || 'Failed to join track.';
      btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Join Track 1: Image Tagging';
    }
  } catch(e) {
    msg.style.display = 'block';
    msg.style.background = '#f8d7da'; msg.style.color = '#721c24';
    msg.textContent = 'Could not reach the server. Is ka_auth_server.py running?';
    btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Join Track 1: Image Tagging';
  }
}
// Show current track if already joined
(function() {
  try {
    const u = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ka_current_user') || '{}');
    if (u.track === 'track1' || u.trackChoice1 === 'track1') {
      const msg = document.getElementById('join-track-msg');
      msg.style.display = 'block'; msg.style.background = '#d4edda'; msg.style.color = '#155724';
      msg.innerHTML = '&#10003; You are currently in Track 1: Image Tagging';
      const btn = document.getElementById('join-track-btn');
      btn.textContent = 'Switch to Track 1 (already joined)'; btn.style.background = '#27ae60';
    }
  } catch(e) {}
})();
</script>
