<!-- ABOUT SECTION -->
<section class="about" id="about">
  <div class="about-inner">
    <div class="section-eyebrow">What is Knowledge Atlas?</div>
    <h2 class="section-title">A knowledge system built on<br>rigorous epistemic foundations</h2>

    <p class="about-lead">
      Knowledge Atlas is not a search engine, a chatbot, or a literature database. It is a
      <strong>coherentist knowledge representation system</strong> — a structured network of
      beliefs, evidence nodes, warrants, and defeat conditions — designed to make the
      epistemic state of a scientific field legible, queryable, and improvable.
    </p>
    <p class="about-body">
      Every claim in Knowledge Atlas carries an explicit credence value, a provenance chain traceable
      to primary sources, and a set of warrant relationships that formalize why and to what degree
      that evidence supports the belief it is linked to. When evidence conflicts, the system does not
      average or suppress — it represents the conflict structurally and surfaces it to the user.
      When evidence is absent, the Value of Information framework quantifies exactly what a new study
      would be worth, making research prioritization a principled calculation rather than a guess.
    </p>
    <p class="about-body">
      The system is built for human factors and cognitive science research, but its epistemic
      architecture is domain-general. The same machinery that evaluates evidence on workplace
      lighting and attention can, in principle, represent any field where controlled studies
      accumulate toward contested theoretical claims.
    </p>

    <!-- THEORY PILLARS -->
    <div id="theory" style="margin-top:52px;">
      <div class="section-eyebrow">Theoretical Architecture</div>
      <h2 class="section-title" style="font-size:1.6rem; margin-bottom:10px;">Five frameworks, unified</h2>
      <p class="about-body" style="margin-bottom:0;">
        Knowledge Atlas draws on five distinct intellectual traditions. Each contributes a different
        structural layer to the system. The author established formal proofs that these frameworks
        are mutually consistent — a non-trivial result given that they were developed independently,
        in different research communities, using different formalisms.
      </p>
    </div>

    <div class="pillars">

      <div class="pillar">
        <div class="pillar-icon">🕸️</div>
        <div class="pillar-name">Coherence Theory of Justification</div>
        <div class="pillar-authors">Thagard · BonJour · Haack</div>
        <div class="pillar-desc">
          Beliefs are justified not by their derivation from foundational axioms but by their
          coherence with the overall web of belief. Knowledge Atlas operationalizes coherence
          as a scored graph property: beliefs with greater mutual support and fewer contradictions
          receive higher credence.
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="pillar">
        <div class="pillar-icon">⚖️</div>
        <div class="pillar-name">Defeasible Warrant &amp; Entrenchment</div>
        <div class="pillar-authors">Pollock · Spohn · Cartwright · Mayo</div>
        <div class="pillar-desc">
          Evidence does not entail conclusions — it <em>warrants</em> them, defeasibly.
          Every evidence-to-belief link carries a typed bridge warrant
          (constitutive, mechanism, empirical association, functional, capacity,
          analogical, or theory-derived), a strength score decomposed into severity,
          replication, confound risk, and source quality, and an explicit defeat
          condition. Public Atlas pages display the canonical bridge type; extraction-layer
          claim classes are tracked separately in detailed views rather than being confused
          with the warrant taxonomy itself.
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="pillar">
        <div class="pillar-icon">🔢</div>
        <div class="pillar-name">Bayesian Belief Networks</div>
        <div class="pillar-authors">Pearl · Jensen · Koller &amp; Friedman</div>
        <div class="pillar-desc">
          The belief network is implemented as a Bayesian graphical model, enabling
          probabilistic propagation of evidence updates. Conditional independence
          assumptions are stated explicitly, and the network supports both forward
          inference (what does this evidence imply?) and backward inference (what evidence
          would most change this belief?).
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="pillar">
        <div class="pillar-icon">🗣️</div>
        <div class="pillar-name">Argumentation Theory</div>
        <div class="pillar-authors">Walton · Dung · Bench-Capon</div>
        <div class="pillar-desc">
          Conflicts between evidence nodes are represented as argumentation frameworks
          with explicit attack and support relations. The acceptability semantics
          (grounded, preferred, stable extensions) determine which beliefs survive
          under a given set of incoming attacks — making the system's conflict resolution
          transparent and auditable.
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="pillar">
        <div class="pillar-icon">📊</div>
        <div class="pillar-name">Value of Information Theory</div>
        <div class="pillar-authors">Howard · Good · Lindley</div>
        <div class="pillar-desc">
          The VOI framework quantifies the expected reduction in decision uncertainty
          that a new observation would produce. Knowledge Atlas uses VOI scores to
          rank research gaps by epistemic priority, making it possible to identify
          exactly which missing studies would most improve the overall coherence
          and decision-relevance of the knowledge base.
        </div>
      </div>

    </div>

    <!-- CONTRIBUTION BLOCK -->
    <div class="contribution">
      <div class="contribution-inner">
        <div class="contrib-eyebrow">The Author's Contribution</div>
        <h3 class="contrib-title">New proofs establishing formal consistency<br>across five independent frameworks</h3>
        <p class="contrib-body">
          Each of the five frameworks above was developed in isolation, in different research
          communities, using different mathematical formalisms. Their simultaneous deployment
          in a single computational system raises a non-trivial question: are they mutually
          consistent? Do they make incompatible demands on how credence should propagate,
          how defeat should be handled, or how information value should be calculated?
        </p>
        <p class="contrib-body">
          The author established a series of original proofs addressing exactly these questions.
          The proofs show that under the specific bridge conditions implemented in Knowledge Atlas,
          the five frameworks do not merely coexist — they reinforce each other. Coherence scores
          constrain Bayesian priors in a principled way. Warrant types determine the functional
          form of the likelihood update. Argumentation-theoretic defeat conditions map cleanly
          onto Bayesian network d-separation. And VOI calculations are grounded in the same
          credence values that the coherence and warrant layers produce.
        </p>

        <ul class="proof-list">
          <li>
            <span class="proof-num">1</span>
            <span><strong>Coherence–Bayes bridge:</strong> Thagard-style coherence maximization converges to the same steady-state credence distribution as Bayesian updating from a uniform prior, given equivalent evidence. The proof establishes the translation function between the two update mechanisms.</span>
          </li>
          <li>
            <span class="proof-num">2</span>
            <span><strong>Warrant–likelihood correspondence:</strong> Each bridge-layer warrant type (constitutive, mechanism, empirical association, functional, capacity, analogical, theory-derived) maps to a distinct likelihood-ratio profile. The proof characterizes these profiles and shows they are formally distinct rather than merely heuristic labels.</span>
          </li>
          <li>
            <span class="proof-num">3</span>
            <span><strong>Defeat–d-separation equivalence:</strong> Undercutting defeat in the argumentation layer is formally equivalent to the introduction of a blocking variable that induces d-separation in the Bayesian network. Rebutting defeat corresponds to the introduction of a contradictory node. The proof shows the two representations are interchangeable without information loss.</span>
          </li>
          <li>
            <span class="proof-num">4</span>
            <span><strong>VOI–coherence monotonicity:</strong> Under the bridge conditions established above, VOI scores are monotonically related to the coherence gap they would close. This means gap prioritization by VOI and prioritization by coherence improvement are equivalent orderings — a consistency result that validates using either metric interchangeably for research planning.</span>
          </li>
        </ul>

        <div class="stats-row">
          <div class="stat">
            <div class="stat-num" id="home-live-topics">--</div>
            <div class="stat-label">Live topics<br>in current payload</div>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <div class="stat-num" id="home-live-articles">--</div>
            <div class="stat-label">Articles currently<br>surfaced in KA</div>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <div class="stat-num" id="home-live-evidence">--</div>
            <div class="stat-label">Evidence rows<br>in current bridge</div>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <div class="stat-num" id="home-live-abstracts">--</div>
            <div class="stat-label">Articles with good<br>abstract coverage</div>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <div class="stat-num" id="home-live-subjects">--</div>
            <div class="stat-label">Articles with good<br>subject-count coverage</div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div class="section-eyebrow" style="margin-top:34px;">Operational Layers</div>
        <h2 class="section-title" style="font-size:1.5rem; margin-bottom:10px;">Four epistemic inspector pages</h2>
        <p class="about-body" style="margin-bottom:22px;">
          Knowledge Atlas is not just article cards and topic lists. The site exposes the warrant, argumentation, annotation, and interpretation layers directly so you can inspect how claims are supported, what has been flagged, what frontier questions remain, and how changing a warrant weight would propagate through the network. Each layer inspector has a Critique and Support explorer for any selected claim.
        </p>

        <div class="pillars">
          <a href="ka_warrants.html" class="pillar" style="text-decoration:none; color:inherit;">
            <div class="pillar-icon">⚖️</div>
            <div class="pillar-name">Warrants Inspector</div>
            <div class="pillar-authors">7 warrant types · sensitivity simulator</div>
            <div class="pillar-desc">
              Inspect the seven warrant types (constitutive to theory-derived), adjust discount multipliers with the sensitivity slider, and see which claims are most affected by changing a theory weight.
            </div>
          </a>

          <a href="ka_argumentation.html" class="pillar" style="text-decoration:none; color:inherit;">
            <div class="pillar-icon">🕸️</div>
            <div class="pillar-name">Argumentation Layer</div>
            <div class="pillar-authors"><span id="home-layer-argumentation">--</span> support edges · <a href="docs/ARGUMENTATION_LAYER_ONE_PAGER_2026-03-26.md">brief</a></div>
            <div class="pillar-desc">
              The support and conflict structure of the corpus. Use the Critique Explorer to see how any claim has been attacked and where its vulnerabilities lie, or the Support Explorer to see what backs it and what would strengthen it further.
            </div>
          </a>

          <a href="ka_annotations.html" class="pillar" style="text-decoration:none; color:inherit;">
            <div class="pillar-icon">📝</div>
            <div class="pillar-name">Annotation Layer</div>
            <div class="pillar-authors"><span id="home-layer-annotations">--</span> active annotations · <a href="docs/ANNOTATION_LAYER_ONE_PAGER_2026-03-26.md">brief</a></div>
            <div class="pillar-desc">
              The review overlay for calibration notes, replication flags, sensitivity warnings, and other signals that help keep weak beliefs from being overpromoted.
            </div>
          </a>

          <a href="ka_interpretation.html" class="pillar" style="text-decoration:none; color:inherit;">
            <div class="pillar-icon">🧭</div>
            <div class="pillar-name">Interpretation Layer</div>
            <div class="pillar-authors"><span id="home-layer-interpretation">--</span> high-VOI questions · <a href="docs/INTERPRETATION_LAYER_ONE_PAGER_2026-03-26.md">brief</a></div>
            <div class="pillar-desc">
              The planning surface that shows active-boundary beliefs, frontier questions, and where the field remains strategically incomplete.
            </div>
          </a>
        </div>

      </div>
    </div>

  </div>
</section>

<script>
(function() {
  const HOME_MODE_COPY = {
    student_explorer: {
      navOrder: ['nav-home-explore', 'nav-home-about', 'nav-home-theory', 'nav-home-docs'],
      primary: { text: 'Explore Topics →', href: 'ka_topics.html' },
      secondary: { text: 'Get Started as a Student', href: 'ka_register.html?student=1' },
      note: 'Student mode foregrounds topics, evidence, and course entry points so the literature becomes the first thing to explore.'
    },
    researcher: {
      navOrder: ['nav-home-explore', 'nav-home-theory', 'nav-home-docs', 'nav-home-about'],
      primary: { text: 'Search the Literature →', href: 'ka_topics.html' },
      secondary: { text: 'Inspect Evidence', href: 'ka_evidence.html' },
      note: 'Researcher mode foregrounds literature exploration, evidence, and theory-linked routes.'
    },
    contributor: {
      navOrder: ['nav-home-docs', 'nav-home-explore', 'nav-home-about', 'nav-home-theory'],
      primary: { text: 'Open Contributor Setup →', href: '160sp/ka_student_setup.html' },
      secondary: { text: 'Register as a Contributor', href: 'ka_register.html' },
      note: 'Contributor mode foregrounds onboarding, setup, and the paths that lead into track work.'
    },
    instructor: {
      navOrder: ['nav-home-docs', 'nav-home-about', 'nav-home-explore', 'nav-home-theory'],
      primary: { text: 'Open Course Hub →', href: '160sp/ka_student_setup.html' },
      secondary: { text: 'Spring Schedule', href: '160sp/ka_schedule.html' },
      note: 'Instructor mode foregrounds course, onboarding, and shared documentation before deep literature tools.'
    },
    practitioner: {
      navOrder: ['nav-home-explore', 'nav-home-about', 'nav-home-docs', 'nav-home-theory'],
      primary: { text: 'Browse Practical Topics →', href: 'ka_topics.html' },
      secondary: { text: 'See Evidence Summaries', href: 'ka_evidence.html' },
      note: 'Practitioner mode foregrounds applied topic browsing and readable evidence, not theory first.'
    },
    theory_mechanism_explorer: {
      navOrder: ['nav-home-theory', 'nav-home-explore', 'nav-home-docs', 'nav-home-about'],
      primary: { text: 'Open Theory Guides →', href: '../theory_guides/index.html' },
      secondary: { text: 'Explore Topics', href: 'ka_topics.html' },
      note: 'Theory Explorer foregrounds explanatory frameworks while keeping literature exploration one click away.'
    }
  };

  var isLoggedIn = !!(localStorage.getItem('ka_access_token') && localStorage.getItem('ka_current_user'));

  function applyHomeMode(mode) {
    const cfg = HOME_MODE_COPY[mode] || HOME_MODE_COPY.student_explorer;
    const nav = document.querySelector('.nav-public');
    const loginBtn = document.querySelector('.btn-login');
    cfg.navOrder.forEach(function(id) {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el) nav.insertBefore(el, loginBtn);
    });

    const primary = document.getElementById('home-primary-cta');
    primary.textContent = cfg.primary.text;
    primary.href = cfg.primary.href;

    const secondary = document.getElementById('home-secondary-cta');
    // If logged in, send to A0 upload instead of registration
    if (isLoggedIn && cfg.secondary.href.includes('ka_register')) {
      secondary.textContent = 'Go to Assignment 0 →';
      secondary.href = '160sp/collect-articles-upload.html';
    } else {
      secondary.textContent = cfg.secondary.text;
      secondary.href = cfg.secondary.href;
    }

    document.getElementById('home-mode-note').textContent = cfg.note;
  }

  window.KA_MODE_SWITCH.initModeControls({
    pillContainerId: 'home-mode-pills',
    onApply: applyHomeMode,
    defaultMode: 'student_explorer'
  });
})();
</script>
<script>
(function() {
  if (!window.KA_PAYLOADS) return;

  function setText(id, value) {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el) el.textContent = String(value);
  }

  Promise.all([
    window.KA_PAYLOADS.loadWithFallback('data/ka_payloads/topics.json', { topics: [] }),
    window.KA_PAYLOADS.loadWithFallback('data/ka_payloads/articles.json', { articles: [] }),
    window.KA_PAYLOADS.loadWithFallback('data/ka_payloads/evidence.json', { evidence: [] }),
    window.KA_PAYLOADS.loadWithFallback('data/ka_payloads/json_status.json', { summary: {} }),
    window.KA_PAYLOADS.loadWithFallback('data/ka_payloads/layers.json', { layers: [] })
  ]).then(function(results) {
    const topics = results[0] || {};
    const articles = results[1] || {};
    const evidence = results[2] || {};
    const jsonStatus = results[3] || {};
    const layers = results[4] || {};
    const summary = jsonStatus.summary || {};
    const layerMap = {};
    (layers.layers || []).forEach(function(layer) { layerMap[layer.id] = layer; });

    setText('home-live-topics', (topics.topics || []).length);
    setText('home-live-articles', (articles.articles || []).length);
    setText('home-live-evidence', (evidence.evidence || []).length);
    setText('home-live-abstracts', summary.abstract_good ?? '--');
    setText('home-live-subjects', summary.subject_count_good ?? '--');
    setText('home-layer-argumentation', layerMap.argumentation ? layerMap.argumentation.primary_metric : '--');
    setText('home-layer-annotations', layerMap.annotations ? layerMap.annotations.primary_metric : '--');
    setText('home-layer-interpretation', layerMap.interpretation ? layerMap.interpretation.primary_metric : '--');
  }).catch(function() {
    setText('home-live-topics', '--');
    setText('home-live-articles', '--');
    setText('home-live-evidence', '--');
    setText('home-live-abstracts', '--');
    setText('home-live-subjects', '--');
    setText('home-layer-argumentation', '--');
    setText('home-layer-annotations', '--');
    setText('home-layer-interpretation', '--');
  });
})();
</script>

        <input type="password" id="login-password" placeholder="Your ATLAS password" autocomplete="current-password" style="padding-right:2.5rem;" />

<script src="ka_workflows.js"></script>

<script src="ka_article_collector.js"></script>
<script>
(function () {
  'use strict';

  const KA_AUTH_API = window.__KA_CONFIG__?.apiBase ?? '';

  /* ── User / Auth State ───────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  let currentUser = null;
  let currentRole = 'student_explorer';
  function togglePwdVis(btn) {
    var inp = btn.parentElement.querySelector('input');
    if (inp.type === 'password') { inp.type = 'text'; btn.innerHTML = '&#128064;'; }
    else { inp.type = 'password'; btn.innerHTML = '&#128065;'; }
  }
  let demoMode = false;

  function loadUser() {
    const token = localStorage.getItem('ka_access_token');
    const stored = localStorage.getItem('ka_current_user');
    if (stored) {
      try { currentUser = JSON.parse(stored); } catch (e) { currentUser = null; }
    }
    if (!token && !stored) {
      // Check URL param for role (for demo / exploration)
      const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      const urlRole = params.get('role');
      if (urlRole && window.KA_WORKFLOWS.roleMeta[urlRole]) {
        currentRole = urlRole;
        demoMode = true;
      } else {
        // Show login overlay
        document.getElementById('login-overlay').style.display = 'flex';
        demoMode = true; // default to demo so overlay can be dismissed
      }
    } else {
      document.getElementById('login-overlay').style.display = 'none';
    }

    // Derive role from user object or localStorage
    if (currentUser) {
      const track = currentUser.track || currentUser.trackChoice1 || '';
      if (currentUser.role === 'instructor' || currentUser.role === 'admin') {
        currentRole = 'instructor';
      } else if (track.toLowerCase().includes('gui')) {
        currentRole = 'student_explorer'; // GUI track students use student mode
      } else {
        currentRole = localStorage.getItem('ka_user_role') || 'student_explorer';
      }
    }
  }

  /* ── Top Bar ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  function renderTopBar() {
    const meta = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.roleMeta[currentRole];
    if (currentUser || !demoMode) {
      let name = 'Demo User';
      if (currentUser) {
        const fn = currentUser.first_name || currentUser.firstName || '';
        const ln = currentUser.last_name || currentUser.lastName || '';
        name = (fn + ' ' + ln).trim() || currentUser.name || currentUser.email || 'Researcher';
      }
      document.getElementById('top-bar-name').textContent = name;
      // Show track badge if available
      const track = currentUser ? (currentUser.track || currentUser.trackChoice1 || '') : '';
      const trackNames = { track1: 'Track 1: Image Tagging', track2: 'Track 2: Article Pipeline', track3: 'Track 3: VR', track4: 'Track 4: Interaction Design' };
      const trackBadge = document.getElementById('top-bar-track-badge');
      if (trackBadge && track && trackNames[track]) {
        trackBadge.textContent = trackNames[track];
        trackBadge.style.display = 'inline-block';
      }
      document.getElementById('top-bar-role-badge').textContent = meta ? meta.label : '';
      document.getElementById('top-bar-role-badge').style.display = 'inline-block';
      document.getElementById('top-bar-logout').style.display = 'inline-block';
      document.getElementById('top-bar-login-btn').style.display = 'none';
    }
  }

  /* ── Sidebar ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  function renderSidebar(role) {
    const meta = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.roleMeta[role];
    if (!meta) return;

    // Role block
    document.getElementById('sidebar-role-icon').textContent = meta.icon;
    document.getElementById('sidebar-role-label').textContent = meta.label;
    document.getElementById('sidebar-role-tagline').textContent = meta.tagline;
    const roleBlock = document.getElementById('sidebar-role-block');
    roleBlock.style.setProperty('--role-color', meta.color);
    roleBlock.style.setProperty('--role-bg', meta.bgLight);
    roleBlock.style.borderColor = meta.color + '55';

    // Workflow nav
    const nav = document.getElementById('sidebar-workflow-nav');
    const wfIds = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.byRole[role] || [];
    nav.innerHTML = wfIds.map(function (id) {
      const wf = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.workflows[id];
      if (!wf) return '';
      const progress = getWorkflowProgress(id);
      const done = progress ? progress.currentStep : 0;
      const total = wf.steps.length;
      return '<a class="wf-nav-item" href="ka_workflow_hub.html?wf=' + id + '">' +
        '<span class="wf-nav-icon">' + wf.icon + '</span>' +
        '<span>' + wf.title + '</span>' +
        (done > 0 ? '<span class="wf-nav-badge">' + done + '/' + total + '</span>' : '') +
      '</a>';
    }).join('');

    const recoveryLink = document.getElementById('sidebar-instructor-recovery-link');
    if (recoveryLink) {
      recoveryLink.style.display = role === 'instructor' ? 'block' : 'none';
    }
  }

  /* ── Role Switcher ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  function renderRoleSwitcher() {
    const row = document.getElementById('role-switcher-row');
    const roles = Object.keys(window.KA_WORKFLOWS.roleMeta);
    row.innerHTML = roles.map(function (r) {
      const meta = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.roleMeta[r];
      const isActive = r === currentRole;
      return '<button class="role-switch-btn' + (isActive ? ' active' : '') + '"' +
        ' data-role="' + r + '"' +
        ' style="' + (isActive ? '--role-color:' + meta.color : '') + '">' +
        meta.icon + ' ' + meta.label +
      '</button>';
    }).join('');

    row.querySelectorAll('.role-switch-btn').forEach(function (btn) {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
        switchRole(btn.dataset.role);
      });
    });

    // Hide role switcher if user is logged in with a fixed role
    if (currentUser && !demoMode) {
      document.getElementById('role-switcher-section').style.display = 'none';
    }
  }

  function switchRole(role) {
    currentRole = role;
    localStorage.setItem('ka_user_role', role);
    render(role);
    // Update URL without reload
    const url = new URL(window.location.href);
    url.searchParams.set('role', role);
    history.replaceState(null, '', url.toString());
  }

  /* ── Welcome ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  function renderWelcome(role) {
    const meta = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.roleMeta[role];
    if (!meta) return;
    const name = currentUser ? (currentUser.name || currentUser.email).split('@')[0] : null;
    document.getElementById('welcome-name').textContent =
      name ? 'Welcome back, ' + name : 'Welcome to ATLAS';
    document.getElementById('welcome-desc').textContent = meta.description;
    document.getElementById('path-guidance-body').textContent =
      'Choose a path for the job you want to do. Follow Next and Back for guidance, or leave the path at any time. Atlas remembers your place.';
  }

  /* ── Resume Card ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  function getWorkflowProgress(wfId) {
    try {
      return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ka_wf_progress_' + wfId) || 'null');
    } catch (e) { return null; }
  }

  function renderResumeCard(role) {
    const wfIds = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.byRole[role] || [];
    let latestProgress = null;
    let latestWfId = null;
    let latestTime = 0;

    wfIds.forEach(function (id) {
      const p = getWorkflowProgress(id);
      if (p && p.lastVisited > latestTime) {
        latestTime = p.lastVisited;
        latestProgress = p;
        latestWfId = id;
      }
    });

    const section = document.getElementById('resume-card-section');
    if (!latestProgress || !latestWfId) { section.style.display = 'none'; return; }

    const wf = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.workflows[latestWfId];
    if (!wf) { section.style.display = 'none'; return; }

    const stepIdx = Math.min(latestProgress.currentStep, wf.steps.length - 1);
    const step = wf.steps[stepIdx];
    section.style.display = 'block';
    document.getElementById('resume-icon').textContent = wf.icon;
    document.getElementById('resume-title').textContent = wf.title;
    document.getElementById('resume-step').textContent =
      'Step ' + (stepIdx + 1) + ' of ' + wf.steps.length + ': ' + (step ? step.title : '');
    document.getElementById('resume-btn').href = 'ka_workflow_hub.html?wf=' + latestWfId + '&step=' + stepIdx;
  }

  /* ── Workflow Grid ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  function renderWorkflowGrid(role) {
    const grid = document.getElementById('workflow-grid');
    const meta = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.roleMeta[role];
    const wfIds = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.byRole[role] || [];

    document.getElementById('workflow-section-heading').textContent =
      meta ? meta.label + ' paths' : 'Recommended paths';

    grid.innerHTML = wfIds.map(function (id) {
      const wf = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.workflows[id];
      if (!wf) return '';
      const progress = getWorkflowProgress(id);
      const done = progress ? Math.min(progress.currentStep, wf.steps.length) : 0;
      const totalSteps = wf.steps.length;
      const isStarted = done > 0;
      const isComplete = done >= totalSteps;

      const pips = wf.steps.map(function (_, i) {
        return '<div class="wf-step-pip' + (i < done ? ' done' : '') + '"' +
          ' style="' + (i < done ? '--wf-color:' + wf.badgeColor : '') + '"></div>';
      }).join('');
      const firstStep = wf.steps[0];
      const lastStep = wf.steps[wf.steps.length - 1];

      return '<a href="ka_workflow_hub.html?wf=' + id + '" class="workflow-card" style="--wf-color:' + wf.badgeColor + '">' +
        '<div class="wf-card-header">' +
          '<div class="wf-card-icon">' + wf.icon + '</div>' +
          '<div class="wf-card-meta">' +
            '<div class="wf-card-badge" style="background:' + wf.badgeColor + '">' + wf.badge + '</div>' +
            '<div class="wf-card-title">' + wf.title + '</div>' +
            '<div class="wf-card-subtitle">' + wf.subtitle + '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="wf-card-objective">' + wf.objective + '</div>' +
        '<div class="wf-card-journey">' +
          '<div class="wf-card-journey-row">' +
            '<span class="wf-journey-pill">Starts at: ' + (firstStep ? firstStep.pageName : 'Atlas') + '</span>' +
            '<span class="wf-journey-pill">Ends at: ' + (lastStep ? lastStep.pageName : 'Atlas') + '</span>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="wf-card-first-step">First page: ' + (firstStep ? firstStep.title + ' on ' + firstStep.pageName : 'Atlas') + '.</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="wf-card-steps-preview">' + pips + '</div>' +
        '<div class="wf-card-footer">' +
          '<span class="wf-card-time">⏱ ' + wf.estimatedTime + ' · ' + totalSteps + ' steps</span>' +
          '<span class="wf-card-cta">' +
            (
              isComplete
                ? 'Review path ✓'
                : isStarted
                  ? 'Continue path →'
                  : 'Open path →'
            ) +
          '</span>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</a>';
    }).join('');
  }

  /* ── A0 Assignment Progress ──────────────────────────────────────────── */

  let a0Questions = [];
  let a0ClaimedQuestion = null;

  async function loadA0Questions() {
    try {
      const token = localStorage.getItem('ka_access_token');
      if (!token) return;

      const res = await fetch(KA_AUTH_API + '/api/articles/questions/available', {
        method: 'GET',
        headers: {
          'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        }
      });

      if (!res.ok) {
        console.log('Failed to load A0 questions:', res.status);
        return;
      }

      const data = await res.json();
      a0Questions = data.available || [];
      updateA0QuestionSelector();
      loadA0Claim();
    } catch (e) {
      console.log('Error loading A0 questions:', e);
    }
  }

  function updateA0QuestionSelector() {
    const selector = document.getElementById('a0-question-selector');
    if (!selector) return;

    const currentValue = selector.value;
    selector.innerHTML = a0Questions.map(function (q) {
      const coverage = q.coverage || {};
      const label = q.label + ' (' + (a0Questions.length - coverage.times_claimed) + ' left)';
      return '<option value="' + q.question_id + '">' + label + '</option>';
    }).join('');

    if (currentValue && a0Questions.find(function (q) { return q.question_id === currentValue; })) {
      selector.value = currentValue;
    } else if (a0Questions.length > 0) {
      selector.value = a0Questions[0].question_id;
    }

    selector.addEventListener('change', updateA0QuestionDisplay);
    updateA0QuestionDisplay();
  }

  function updateA0QuestionDisplay() {
    const selector = document.getElementById('a0-question-selector');
    const qId = selector.value;
    const q = a0Questions.find(function (q) { return q.question_id === qId; });

    const display = document.getElementById('a0-question-display');
    if (!q || a0ClaimedQuestion) {
      display.style.display = 'none';
    } else {
      display.style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('a0-question-title').textContent = q.label;
      document.getElementById('a0-question-text').textContent = q.text;
    }
  }

  async function loadA0Claim() {
    try {
      const token = localStorage.getItem('ka_access_token');
      if (!token) return;

      const res = await fetch(KA_AUTH_API + '/api/articles/questions/my-claim', {
        method: 'GET',
        headers: {
          'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        }
      });

      if (!res.ok) {
        console.log('Failed to load A0 claim:', res.status);
        return;
      }

      const data = await res.json();
      if (data.has_claim && data.claims && data.claims.length > 0) {
        a0ClaimedQuestion = data.claims[0];
        renderA0Progress(a0ClaimedQuestion, data.total_progress);
      } else {
        a0ClaimedQuestion = null;
        document.getElementById('a0-progress-section').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('a0-empty-state').style.display = 'block';
      }
      updateA0UI();
    } catch (e) {
      console.log('Error loading A0 claim:', e);
    }
  }

  function renderA0Progress(claim, totalProgress) {
    const container = document.getElementById('a0-tasks-container');
    const section = document.getElementById('a0-progress-section');

    let html = '';

    // Task 1 (Experimental)
    if (claim.progress && claim.progress.task1) {
      const t1 = claim.progress.task1;
      const pct1 = t1.required > 0 ? Math.round((t1.confirmed_experimental / t1.required) * 100) : 0;
      const isComplete1 = t1.complete;

      html += '<div class="a0-task-block">' +
        '<div class="a0-task-header">' +
          '<span class="a0-task-label">Task 1: Confirm Experimental Articles</span>' +
          '<span class="a0-task-count">' + t1.confirmed_experimental + '/' + t1.required + ' articles</span>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="a0-progress-bar">' +
          '<div class="a0-progress-fill' + (isComplete1 ? '' : ' in-progress') + '" style="width:' + pct1 + '%"></div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="a0-status-pills">' +
          '<span class="a0-status-pill ' + (isComplete1 ? 'confirmed' : 'pending') + '">' +
            (isComplete1 ? '✓ Complete' : '◌ In Progress') +
          '</span>' +
          '<span class="a0-status-pill pending">' + t1.submitted + ' submitted</span>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>';
    }

    // Task 2 (Any Type)
    if (claim.progress && claim.progress.task2) {
      const t2 = claim.progress.task2;
      const pct2 = t2.required > 0 ? Math.round((t2.complete / t2.required) * 100) : 0;
      const isComplete2 = t2.complete >= t2.required;

      html += '<div class="a0-task-block">' +
        '<div class="a0-task-header">' +
          '<span class="a0-task-label">Task 2: Confirm Any-Type Articles</span>' +
          '<span class="a0-task-count">' + t2.complete + '/' + t2.required + ' articles</span>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="a0-progress-bar">' +
          '<div class="a0-progress-fill' + (isComplete2 ? '' : ' in-progress') + '" style="width:' + pct2 + '%"></div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="a0-status-pills">' +
          '<span class="a0-status-pill ' + (isComplete2 ? 'confirmed' : 'pending') + '">' +
            (isComplete2 ? '✓ Complete' : '◌ In Progress') +
          '</span>' +
          '<span class="a0-status-pill pending">' + t2.submitted + ' submitted</span>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>';
    }

    container.innerHTML = html;
    section.style.display = 'block';
    document.getElementById('a0-empty-state').style.display = 'none';
  }

  function updateA0UI() {
    const selector = document.getElementById('a0-question-selector');
    const claimBtn = document.getElementById('a0-claim-btn');
    const releaseBtn = document.getElementById('a0-release-btn');
    const display = document.getElementById('a0-question-display');

    if (a0ClaimedQuestion) {
      selector.disabled = true;
      claimBtn.style.display = 'none';
      releaseBtn.style.display = 'inline-block';
      display.style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('a0-question-title').textContent = a0ClaimedQuestion.label;
      document.getElementById('a0-question-text').textContent = a0ClaimedQuestion.text;
    } else {
      selector.disabled = false;
      claimBtn.style.display = 'inline-block';
      releaseBtn.style.display = 'none';
      display.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }

  async function claimA0Question() {
    try {
      const token = localStorage.getItem('ka_access_token');
      const selector = document.getElementById('a0-question-selector');
      const qId = selector.value;

      if (!token || !qId) return;

      const res = await fetch(KA_AUTH_API + '/api/articles/questions/claim', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ question_id: qId })
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) {
        console.log('Claim failed:', data);
        return;
      }

      loadA0Questions();
      loadA0Claim();
    } catch (e) {
      console.log('Error claiming question:', e);
    }
  }

  async function releaseA0Question() {
    if (!a0ClaimedQuestion) return;

    try {
      const token = localStorage.getItem('ka_access_token');
      if (!token) return;

      const res = await fetch(KA_AUTH_API + '/api/articles/questions/release', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ question_id: a0ClaimedQuestion.question_id })
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) {
        console.log('Release failed:', data);
        return;
      }

      a0ClaimedQuestion = null;
      loadA0Questions();
      loadA0Claim();
    } catch (e) {
      console.log('Error releasing question:', e);
    }
  }

  function initA0() {
    const claimBtn = document.getElementById('a0-claim-btn');
    const releaseBtn = document.getElementById('a0-release-btn');
    const selector = document.getElementById('a0-question-selector');

    if (claimBtn) claimBtn.addEventListener('click', claimA0Question);
    if (releaseBtn) releaseBtn.addEventListener('click', releaseA0Question);
    if (selector) selector.addEventListener('change', updateA0QuestionDisplay);

    loadA0Questions();
  }

  function renderA0Section() {
    const section = document.getElementById('a0-section');
    if (currentUser && !demoMode) {
      section.style.display = 'block';
      initA0();
    } else {
      section.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }

  /* ── Main Render ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  function render(role) {
    renderWelcome(role);
    renderSidebar(role);
    renderRoleSwitcher();
    renderResumeCard(role);
    renderA0Section();
    renderWorkflowGrid(role);

    // For logged-in students: show only A0 progress. Hide role switcher, workflows, guidance.
    const isStudent = currentUser && !demoMode && (role === 'student_explorer' || role === 'student');
    const isInstructor = currentUser && (role === 'instructor' || role === 'admin');
    document.getElementById('path-guidance-section').style.display = (demoMode || isInstructor) ? '' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('role-switcher-section').style.display = demoMode ? '' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('workflow-section-heading').style.display = (demoMode || isInstructor) ? '' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('workflow-grid').style.display = (demoMode || isInstructor) ? '' : 'none';

    // Update active state in role switcher
    document.querySelectorAll('.role-switch-btn').forEach(function (btn) {
      const meta = window.KA_WORKFLOWS.roleMeta[btn.dataset.role];
      btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.role === role);
      if (btn.dataset.role === role && meta) {
        btn.style.setProperty('--role-color', meta.color);
        btn.style.background = meta.color;
        btn.style.borderColor = meta.color;
        btn.style.color = '#fff';
      } else {
        btn.style.background = '';
        btn.style.borderColor = '';
        btn.style.color = '';
      }
    });
  }

  /* ── Login ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  function initLogin() {
    const btn = document.getElementById('login-submit-btn');
    const demoBtn = document.getElementById('login-demo-btn');
    const errorEl = document.getElementById('login-error');

    btn.addEventListener('click', async function () {
      const email = document.getElementById('login-email').value.trim();
      const password = document.getElementById('login-password').value;
      if (!email || !password) { showError('Please enter both email and password.'); return; }

      btn.textContent = 'Logging in…';
      btn.disabled = true;

      try {
        const res = await fetch(KA_AUTH_API + '/auth/login', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ email, password })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (!res.ok) { showError(data.detail || 'Login failed.'); btn.textContent = 'Log in →'; btn.disabled = false; return; }

        localStorage.setItem('ka_access_token', data.access_token);
        localStorage.setItem('ka_current_user', JSON.stringify(data.user));
        localStorage.setItem('ka_logged_in', '1');
        currentUser = data.user;
        demoMode = false;  // Exit demo mode on successful login
        document.getElementById('login-overlay').style.display = 'none';
        loadUser();
        renderTopBar();
        render(currentRole);
      } catch (e) {
        // Auth server not reachable — offer demo mode
        showError('Auth server not reachable. Use demo mode to continue.');
        btn.textContent = 'Log in →'; btn.disabled = false;
      }
    });

    demoBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
      demoMode = true;
      document.getElementById('login-overlay').style.display = 'none';
      render(currentRole);
    });

    document.getElementById('top-bar-login-btn').addEventListener('click', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      document.getElementById('login-overlay').style.display = 'flex';
    });

    document.getElementById('top-bar-logout').addEventListener('click', function () {
      localStorage.removeItem('ka_access_token');
      localStorage.removeItem('ka_current_user');
      localStorage.removeItem('ka_logged_in');
      currentUser = null;
      demoMode = true;
      renderTopBar();
      render(currentRole);
    });

    function showError(msg) {
      errorEl.textContent = msg;
      errorEl.style.display = 'block';
    }
  }

  /* ── Boot ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  function boot() {
    loadUser();
    renderTopBar();
    render(currentRole);
    initLogin();
    window.KA_COLLECTOR.init();
  }

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', boot);
  } else {
    boot();
  }

})();
</script>

// Class intro CTA — injected via JS to avoid HTML nesting issues
window.addEventListener('load', function() {
  var footer = document.querySelector('footer') || document.querySelector('.ka-page-footer');
  var target = footer || document.body;
  if (!document.getElementById('class-intro-cta')) {
    var cta = document.createElement('div');
    cta.id = 'class-intro-cta';
    cta.style.cssText = 'text-align:center; padding:40px 20px 20px;';
    cta.innerHTML = '<a href="160sp/ka_schedule.html" style="display:inline-block; background:#1C3D3A; color:#F7F4EF; font-size:1.1rem; font-weight:700; padding:14px 36px; border-radius:8px; text-decoration:none; letter-spacing:0.3px; border:2px solid #E8872A; box-shadow:0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.15);">← Back to Schedule</a>';
    if (footer) {
      footer.parentNode.insertBefore(cta, footer);
    } else {
      document.body.appendChild(cta);
    }
  }
});
</script>

    <script>
    // ── Real JWT auth (requires ka_auth_server.py running on port 8765)
    const KA_AUTH_API = window.__KA_CONFIG__?.apiBase ?? '';

    // Show an error banner under the form
    function showLoginError(msg) {
      let el = document.getElementById('ka-login-error');
      if (!el) {
        el = document.createElement('div');
        el.id = 'ka-login-error';
        el.style.cssText = 'background:#FEE2E2;border:1px solid #FCA5A5;color:#7F1D1D;' +
          'border-radius:6px;padding:11px 14px;font-size:.85rem;margin-top:12px;line-height:1.5';
        document.querySelector('#loginForm button[type=submit]').after(el);
      }
      el.textContent = msg;
      el.style.display = 'block';
    }
    function clearLoginError() {
      const el = document.getElementById('ka-login-error');
      if (el) el.style.display = 'none';
    }

    document.getElementById('loginForm').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      clearLoginError();
      const email    = document.getElementById('email').value.trim();
      const password = document.getElementById('password').value;
      const btn      = this.querySelector('button[type=submit]');
      btn.disabled   = true;
      btn.textContent = 'Signing in…';

      try {
        const res = await fetch(`${KA_AUTH_API}/auth/login`, {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
          body: JSON.stringify({email, password})
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        if (!res.ok) {
          showLoginError(data.detail || 'Login failed. Check your email and password.');
          btn.disabled = false;
          btn.textContent = 'Sign In';
          return;
        }

        // Store the short-lived access token and user info in localStorage.
        localStorage.setItem('ka_access_token',  data.access_token);
        localStorage.setItem('ka_current_user',  JSON.stringify(data.user));
        localStorage.setItem('ka_logged_in', '1');
        sessionStorage.setItem('ka_logged_in', '1');

        // Backward-compat: keep workflow store in sync
        if (window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE) window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.setLoggedIn(true);

        // Route by role
        const role = data.user.role || 'student';
        if (role === 'instructor' || role === 'admin') {
          window.location.href = 'ka_approve.html';
        } else {
          // For students: check A0 completion status
          try {
            const progressRes = await fetch('/api/student/progress/' + encodeURIComponent(data.user.user_id || data.user.email));
            if (progressRes.ok) {
              const progress = await progressRes.json();
              if (progress.a0_complete) {
                window.location.href = '160sp/ka_schedule.html';
              } else {
                window.location.href = '160sp/ka_student_setup.html';
              }
            } else {
              // API not available, default to setup page
              window.location.href = '160sp/ka_student_setup.html';
            }
          } catch(e) {
            // Progress check failed, default to setup page
            console.warn('[KA] Could not check A0 progress:', e);
            window.location.href = '160sp/ka_student_setup.html';
          }
        }

      } catch(ex) {
        // Auth server unreachable — fall back to demo mode
        console.warn('[KA] Auth server not reachable, using demo mode:', ex);
        showLoginError(
          'Auth server not reachable (is ka_auth_server.py running?). ' +
          'Falling back to demo mode — click Sign In again to continue.'
        );
        // Second click: proceed with demo mode
        btn.textContent = 'Continue in demo mode →';
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.onclick = function() {
          localStorage.setItem('ka_logged_in', '1');
          sessionStorage.setItem('ka_logged_in', '1');
          if (window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE) window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.setLoggedIn(true);
          const dest = email.includes('instructor') || email.includes('prof')
            ? 'ka_approve.html' : 'ka_user_home.html';
          window.location.href = dest;
        };
      }
    });
    </script>

<script>
window.KA_PAGE_FUNCTION = {
  pageId: 'ka_login',
  title: 'Knowledge Atlas — Login',
  audience: 'Returning contributors, students, instructors, and administrators',
  purpose: 'Authenticates returning users and routes them to the appropriate landing page based on role: students go to the dashboard, contributors to the tagger or articles page, instructors to the approval and review queue. Currently a static form; requires JWT authentication backend to function.',
  workflowPos: 'Gate before any authenticated workflow. The walkthrough uses a DB-backed workflow snapshot plus a browser login overlay so authenticated page affordances can be exercised without a full auth server.',
  notFor: 'New user registration (link to Register page), password reset (separate flow), or any content browsing.',
  phase: 'Phase 1 — Foundation Infrastructure (P0 — blocks all authenticated features)',
  evalQuestions: [
    'Is it immediately clear whether the user should Log In or Register?',
    'Is the role-based routing explained anywhere, or does the user land somewhere confusing?',
    'Is there a visible path back to the home page or demo without logging in?',
    'Does the form give clear error feedback (wrong password, account not yet approved)?',
    'Is the "Instructor Approve" path discoverable for new instructors?'
  ]
};
</script>

    <script>
    // Password show/hide toggle (event listener, not inline onclick)
    document.querySelectorAll('.pwd-eye-btn').forEach(function(btn) {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var inp = this.parentElement.querySelector('input');
        if (inp.type === 'password') { inp.type = 'text'; this.innerHTML = '&#128064;'; }
        else { inp.type = 'password'; this.innerHTML = '&#128065;'; }
      });
    });
    (function() {
      const NAV_PREFERENCE_BY_TYPE = {
        student_explorer: 'explore_literature',
        researcher: 'explore_literature',
        contributor: 'contribute_atlas',
        instructor: 'build_test_experiments',
        practitioner: 'explore_literature',
        theory_mechanism_explorer: 'theory_mechanisms'
      };

      // ── Track label names ────────────────────────────────────────────
      const TRACK_NAMES = {
        track1: 'Track 1 — Image Tagging',
        track2: 'Track 2 — Article Finding',
        track3: 'Track 3 — VR Production',
        track4: 'Track 4 — GUI Evaluation & Experiment Design'
      };
      const KA_AUTH_API = window.__KA_CONFIG__?.apiBase ?? '';
      const duplicateLoginModal = document.getElementById('duplicateLoginModal');
      const duplicateLoginLead = document.getElementById('duplicateLoginLead');
      const duplicateLoginForm = document.getElementById('duplicateLoginForm');
      const duplicateLoginEmail = document.getElementById('duplicateLoginEmail');
      const duplicateLoginPassword = document.getElementById('duplicateLoginPassword');
      const duplicateLoginSubmit = document.getElementById('duplicateLoginSubmit');
      const duplicateLoginMsg = document.getElementById('duplicateLoginMsg');
      const duplicateForgotLink = document.getElementById('duplicateForgotLink');
      const duplicateLoginPageLink = document.getElementById('duplicateLoginPageLink');

      function showDuplicateLoginMessage(message, kind) {
        duplicateLoginMsg.className = 'auth-modal-msg ' + (kind || 'error');
        duplicateLoginMsg.textContent = message;
      }

      function clearDuplicateLoginMessage() {
        duplicateLoginMsg.className = 'auth-modal-msg';
        duplicateLoginMsg.textContent = '';
      }

      function openDuplicateLoginModal(email, leadText) {
        duplicateLoginEmail.value = email || '';
        duplicateLoginPassword.value = '';
        duplicateLoginLead.textContent = leadText || 'That email already has a K-ATLAS account. Sign in here instead of registering again.';
        duplicateForgotLink.href = 'ka_forgot_password.html' + (email ? ('?email=' + encodeURIComponent(email)) : '');
        duplicateLoginPageLink.href = 'ka_login.html' + (email ? ('?email=' + encodeURIComponent(email)) : '');
        clearDuplicateLoginMessage();
        duplicateLoginModal.classList.add('visible');
        duplicateLoginPassword.focus();
      }

      function closeDuplicateLoginModal() {
        duplicateLoginModal.classList.remove('visible');
        duplicateLoginPassword.value = '';
        clearDuplicateLoginMessage();
      }

      duplicateLoginForm.addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        const email = duplicateLoginEmail.value.trim();
        const password = duplicateLoginPassword.value;
        if (!email || !password) return;

        duplicateLoginSubmit.disabled = true;
        duplicateLoginSubmit.textContent = 'Signing In…';
        clearDuplicateLoginMessage();

        try {
          const res = await fetch(KA_AUTH_API + '/auth/login', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ email: email, password: password })
          });
          const data = await res.json();

          if (!res.ok) {
            showDuplicateLoginMessage(data.detail || 'Sign-in failed. Check your password or use password help.', 'error');
            return;
          }

          localStorage.removeItem('katlas_token');
          localStorage.removeItem('katlas_user');
          localStorage.setItem('ka_access_token', data.access_token);
          localStorage.setItem('ka_refresh_token', data.refresh_token);
          localStorage.setItem('ka_current_user', JSON.stringify(data.user));
          localStorage.setItem('ka_logged_in', '1');
          sessionStorage.setItem('ka_logged_in', '1');
          showDuplicateLoginMessage('Sign-in successful. Redirecting…', 'success');
          window.location.href = '160sp/ka_student_setup.html';
        } catch (err) {
          showDuplicateLoginMessage('Could not reach the authentication server. Please try again or use the full sign-in page.', 'error');
        } finally {
          duplicateLoginSubmit.disabled = false;
          duplicateLoginSubmit.textContent = 'Sign In';
        }
      });

      document.getElementById('duplicateLoginClose').addEventListener('click', closeDuplicateLoginModal);
      duplicateLoginModal.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (e.target === duplicateLoginModal) closeDuplicateLoginModal();
      });

      const storedMode = sessionStorage.getItem('ka_active_mode') || localStorage.getItem('ka_user_type');
      if (storedMode && document.getElementById('userTypeChoice')) {
        document.getElementById('userTypeChoice').value = storedMode;
      }

      // ── COGS 160 student checkbox ───────────────────────────────────
      const is160Checkbox = document.getElementById('is160Student');
      const cogs160Note   = document.getElementById('cogs160Note');
      const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      if (urlParams.get('student') === '1') {
        is160Checkbox.checked = true;
        cogs160Note.style.display = 'block';
      }
      is160Checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
        cogs160Note.style.display = this.checked ? 'block' : 'none';
        if (this.checked) {
          document.getElementById('institution').value = document.getElementById('institution').value || 'UC San Diego';
          document.getElementById('department').value = 'COGS 160';
          document.getElementById('roleUG').checked = true;
          document.getElementById('userTypeChoice').value = 'student_explorer';
        }
      });
      // Fire change if pre-checked from URL
      if (is160Checkbox.checked) is160Checkbox.dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));

      // ── Password strength ────────────────────────────────────────────
      const pwInput = document.getElementById('password');
      const pwBar   = document.getElementById('pwBar');
      const pwHint  = document.getElementById('pwHint');

      pwInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
        const v = this.value;
        let score = 0;
        if (v.length >= 8)  score++;
        if (v.length >= 12) score++;
        if (/[A-Z]/.test(v)) score++;
        if (/[0-9]/.test(v)) score++;
        if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(v)) score++;
        const pct = Math.min(100, score * 20);
        pwBar.style.width  = pct + '%';
        const colors = ['#E74C3C','#E74C3C','#E8872A','#F5A623','#2A7868','#2A7868'];
        const labels = ['Too short','Too short','Weak','Fair','Strong','Very strong'];
        pwBar.style.background = colors[score];
        pwHint.textContent = v.length === 0 ? 'At least 8 characters' : labels[score];
        if (v.length > 0 && v.length < 8) {
          showErr('password','Password must be at least 8 characters.');
        } else {
          clearErr('password');
        }
      });

      // ── Inline validation helpers ────────────────────────────────────
      function showErr(id, msg) {
        const el = document.getElementById('err-' + id);
        const inp = document.getElementById(id);
        if (el) { el.textContent = msg; el.classList.add('visible'); }
        if (inp) inp.classList.add('input-error');
      }
      function clearErr(id) {
        const el = document.getElementById('err-' + id);
        const inp = document.getElementById(id);
        if (el) el.classList.remove('visible');
        if (inp) { inp.classList.remove('input-error'); inp.classList.add('input-ok'); }
      }
      function markClean(id) {
        const inp = document.getElementById(id);
        if (inp) { inp.classList.remove('input-error'); inp.classList.add('input-ok'); }
      }

      // ── Real-time blur validation ────────────────────────────────────
      ['firstName','lastName'].forEach(id => {
        document.getElementById(id).addEventListener('blur', function() {
          if (!this.value.trim()) showErr(id, 'This field is required.');
          else clearErr(id);
        });
      });

      document.getElementById('email').addEventListener('blur', function() {
        if (!this.value.trim()) { showErr('email','Email is required.'); return; }
        if (!/^[^@\s]+@[^@\s]+\.[^@\s]+$/.test(this.value)) {
          showErr('email','Please enter a valid email address.');
        } else {
          // Check duplicate in localStorage
          const regs = window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE ? window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.pendingRegistrations() : JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ka_pending_registrations') || '[]');
          const dup = regs.find(r => r.email.toLowerCase() === this.value.toLowerCase());
          if (dup) showErr('email', 'An account with this email already exists. Submit once and the sign-in window will open.');
          else clearErr('email');
        }
      });

      document.getElementById('confirmPassword').addEventListener('blur', function() {
        const pw = document.getElementById('password').value;
        if (this.value && this.value !== pw) showErr('confirmPassword','Passwords do not match.');
        else if (this.value) clearErr('confirmPassword');
      });

      document.getElementById('trackChoice1').addEventListener('change', function() {
        const name = TRACK_NAMES[this.value] || 'your first-choice track';
        document.getElementById('skills1Label').textContent = 'Relevant skills for ' + name;
        if (this.value) clearErr('trackChoice1');
      });

      // ── Form submission ──────────────────────────────────────────────
      document.getElementById('registerForm').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        let ok = true;

        // Required text fields
        ['firstName','lastName'].forEach(id => {
          const val = document.getElementById(id).value.trim();
          if (!val) { showErr(id, 'This field is required.'); ok = false; }
          else clearErr(id);
        });

        // Email
        const email = document.getElementById('email').value.trim();
        if (!email || !/^[^@\s]+@[^@\s]+\.[^@\s]+$/.test(email)) {
          showErr('email','Please enter a valid email address.'); ok = false;
        } else {
          const regs = window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE ? window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.pendingRegistrations() : JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ka_pending_registrations') || '[]');
          if (regs.find(r => r.email.toLowerCase() === email.toLowerCase())) {
            showErr('email','An account with this email already exists. Use the sign-in window instead.');
            openDuplicateLoginModal(email, 'That email is already registered. Sign in here instead of creating a second account.');
            return;
          } else clearErr('email');
        }

        // Password
        const pw = document.getElementById('password').value;
        if (pw.length < 8) { showErr('password','Password must be at least 8 characters.'); ok = false; }
        else clearErr('password');

        // Confirm password
        const cpw = document.getElementById('confirmPassword').value;
        if (cpw !== pw) { showErr('confirmPassword','Passwords do not match.'); ok = false; }
        else if (cpw) clearErr('confirmPassword');

        // Track choice
        const track1 = document.getElementById('trackChoice1').value;
        if (!track1) { showErr('trackChoice1','Please select a first-choice track.'); ok = false; }
        else clearErr('trackChoice1');

        if (!ok) {
          // Scroll to first visible error
          const firstErr = document.querySelector('.field-error.visible');
          if (firstErr) firstErr.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
          return;
        }

        // ── All valid: register with the auth server ────────────────────
        const firstName = document.getElementById('firstName').value.trim();
        const lastName  = document.getElementById('lastName').value.trim();
        const department = document.getElementById('department').value.trim();

        const userData = {
          firstName: firstName,
          lastName:  lastName,
          email:     email,
          role:      document.querySelector('input[name="role"]:checked')?.value || 'undergrad',
          institution: document.getElementById('institution').value.trim(),
          department:  department,
          userType: document.getElementById('userTypeChoice').value,
          navPreference: NAV_PREFERENCE_BY_TYPE[document.getElementById('userTypeChoice').value] || 'explore_literature',
          trackChoice1: track1,
          trackChoice2: document.getElementById('trackChoice2').value,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
          status: 'approved'
        };

        // POST to auth server so the account exists in SQLite for login
        let serverRegistered = false;
        let duplicateAccount = false;
        try {
          const is160 = document.getElementById('is160Student').checked;
          const regBody = {
            email:      email,
            password:   pw,
            first_name: firstName,
            last_name:  lastName,
            department: is160 ? 'COGS 160' : department,
            track:      track1
          };
          if (is160) regBody.question_id = 'A0';
          const regRes = await fetch(KA_AUTH_API + '/auth/register', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(regBody)
          });
          const regData = await regRes.json();
          if (regRes.ok) {
            serverRegistered = true;
            userData.id = regData.user_id;
          } else if (regRes.status === 409) {
            duplicateAccount = true;
          } else {
            console.warn('[KA] Server registration returned error:', regData.detail);
          }
        } catch (e) {
          console.warn('[KA] Auth server not reachable, saving locally only:', e);
        }

        if (duplicateAccount) {
          showErr('email','An account with this email already exists. Use the sign-in window instead.');
          openDuplicateLoginModal(email, 'That email is already registered. Sign in with it now, or use password help if you have forgotten the password.');
          return;
        }

        // Fallback: also persist to localStorage for offline/demo use
        if (!userData.id) userData.id = 'student_' + Date.now();
        if (window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE) {
          window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.addPendingRegistration(userData);
          if (window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.approveRegistration) {
            window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.approveRegistration(userData.id, userData.trackChoice1);
          }
        } else {
          const regs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ka_pending_registrations') || '[]');
          regs.push(userData);
          localStorage.setItem('ka_pending_registrations', JSON.stringify(regs));
        }

        // Registration does not create an authenticated session.
        if (window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE) {
          window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.setCurrentUser(null);
          window.KA_WORKFLOW_STORE.setLoggedIn(false);
        }
        localStorage.removeItem('ka_access_token');
        localStorage.removeItem('ka_refresh_token');
        localStorage.removeItem('ka_current_user');
        localStorage.removeItem('ka_logged_in');
        localStorage.removeItem('katlas_token');
        localStorage.removeItem('katlas_user');
        sessionStorage.removeItem('ka_logged_in');
        localStorage.setItem('ka_user_type', userData.userType);
        sessionStorage.setItem('ka_active_mode', userData.userType);

        // ── Show success screen ──────────────────────────────────────────
        const is160Success = document.getElementById('is160Student').checked;
        document.getElementById('registerForm').style.display = 'none';
        const screen = document.getElementById('successScreen');
        screen.classList.add('visible');
        const statusMsg = serverRegistered
          ? 'Active — ready to sign in'
          : 'Saved locally (auth server offline) — sign in when server is running';
        document.getElementById('successDetail').innerHTML =
          '<strong>Name:</strong> ' + userData.firstName + ' ' + userData.lastName + '<br>' +
          '<strong>Email:</strong> ' + userData.email + '<br>' +
          '<strong>Track requested:</strong> ' + (TRACK_NAMES[track1] || track1) + '<br>' +
          '<strong>Status:</strong> ' + statusMsg;

        // 160 students: redirect to sign-in after brief pause
        if (is160Success && serverRegistered) {
          document.getElementById('successDetail').innerHTML +=
            '<br><br>Redirecting to Sign In\u2026';
          setTimeout(function() { window.location.href = 'ka_login.html'; }, 2000);
        }
        screen.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    })();
    </script>
